Sometimes though with how often Agatha flirted with Rio, it was hard for her to remember she wasn’t special. Not that she would be (She wanted to) at all. 

 

“In your dreams” Rio scoffed.

 

“No, not that you perv,” Agatha rolled her eyes, but abruptly planted a smirk on her face with a low, “Unless-”

 

“ Agatha”

 

The woman snorted, tossing her hands up in defense.  

 

“Listen, it’s very clear you need a shoulder to lean on tonight. I mean, come on, Vidal! It’s a Friday night and you’re crying in the goddamn ice cream section!”

 

“You’re here too, you know?” 

 

“I’m not the one covered in tears and grabbing fucking rocky road out of all flavors” She scrunched her nose in disgust. “Jesus, no wonder you’re crying. I would be too eating that shit” 

 

Rio turned from the freezer, her eyes narrowed with lips tugged back out of frustration. Seeing the other professor stride through the university halls, the breakroom to every board meeting, having to hear her name from every single student. And now dealing with her in the middle of the fucking grocery store ? Just when Rio didn’t think this night could get any worse…

 

“Can you go one minute of your life without insulting someone, Agatha ?” Rio glared.

 

“Can you go five minutes without looking at me as if I’m scum of the earth, Professor Vidal ?”

 

Agatha grinned through the name, confirming Rio’s theory on how she couldn’t live without being a nuisance. And yet? Rio still couldn’t ignore what her professional name rolling off Agatha’s tongue did to her. Things that made the warmth between her legs burn, head spiral off its handles. Fuck. She hated her. 

 

“One for five? Shit deal” Rio scoffed. 

 

“Three for three then?” Agatha countered. “And fine, since you take me as someone who sleeps on the first date- We don’t have to go to my place. My car has a good stereo if you just want to blast music till your eardrums bleed”

 

Rio turned, ice cream freezing her skin while watching the way Agatha wiggled her melted one in the air with a disgustingly, far too, overwhelmingly, intriguing grin. 

 

Why are you debating this, Rio?

 

“Why are you so adamant we spend time together?”

 

Rio had to question that more than anything else, including why she was considering accepting Agatha’s offer. After three years of Rio clearly making it known she didn’t care for Agatha, wanted nothing to do with her, couldn’t stand her, all of the above-

 

Why is she asking me this?

 

“Why are you so adamant we don’t?” Agatha countered. 

 

The younger woman didn’t give Rio time to think about her question. Instead she shrugged, voice sinking into a lower depth as if she wanted her words to be sacred for Rio’s ears only. 

 

“The doors won’t be locked,” Agatha said, taking a step forward. A tiny shrug, pout of her lips that curled into a little smirk. “Well, unless you want to get frisky then-”

 

“Jesus Christ!" Rio laughed in disbelief, spinning around on her heel to leave. Just as she was about to exit the aisle?

 

“Rio, come on!” Agatha exclaimed through a laugh. “I don’t bite! Unless you want me to, of course, but..” She added. “Seriously..”

 

Her voice had fallen, no teasing or humor in it. Rio felt her feet slow down, coming to a stop as she heard Agatha’s sigh.

 

“Can we just put aside whatever it is that makes you hate me tonight?”

 

The question made her ache. A tight squeeze in her chest, bringing a pain as if her heart was bruised. She pulled her lips back, holding tighter to the basket’s handles in one hand and pint of ice cream in the other. 

 

Why did Agatha sound exhausted? Especially as she spoke the word, hate. It sounded as if she was pinning all of this on Rio. Sure, maybe she never truly gave Agatha a chance like Lilia begged her to. But, it was the younger woman’s fault for being so damn annoying all the time! 

 

Between the insults, banter, annoyance- No. Agatha had her hand in this feud, divide, enemy stance as well.

 

Rio spun around, eyes narrowed in on her target as she shook her head. 

 

“Don’t make it sound like it’s just me here” She ordered. “You have given me shit. You have insulted me, made my life difficult as all hell. It is not just me here, Agatha”

 

Agatha tilted her head to the left just an inch, lips parted before she whipped back a quick,

 

“Three years, Rio.. ” She said, putting emphasis on the first name she rarely spoke. Always nicknames or her last, but never the first. “You’ve glared, avoided, given me a cold shoul-”

 

“You gifted me a cactus this morning that called me a prick!”

 

“That is a light hearted joke compared to the shit you give me and you know it!” 

 

Rio pulled back, holding her breath as she tried to navigate the situation. No humor was to be found. Not a hint of a joke anywhere she looked. Agatha was serious. Her eyes exhausted, voice low, no teasing or flirts on the horizon. The woman looked…hurt, almost. 

 

She shook her head, desperate to rid the shitty feeling of guilt boiling up within her. Swirling in her stomach, drowning her heart and flooding her throat with more sobs. Not only was she not meant for love, she was a terrible human for making someone feel like shit. 

 

Two for two tonight, good job.

 

Agatha sighed, running a hand through her hair before waving it back in the air. 

 

“Listen,” She said. “You’re sobbing in the ice cream aisle on a Friday night. I’m here begging my enemy to hang out in my fucking car with me. So..”

 

She shrugged, gesturing her hand aggressively between them both. Shaking it as if she was trying to free her words from their restraints. Agatha wouldn’t look at her anymore, Rio took note of it. Either her eyes were closed or they stared elsewhere. And suddenly, she missed those twinkling blue orbs for whatever reason. 

 

What is happening to me?

 

Rio knew lust, infatuation. Both were always there between the layers of resentment and fury. But this? She silently thanked Agatha for breaking the silence again before sinking herself into another pit of turmoil.

 

“Let’s just be pathetic enemies..together. One night only”

 

One night only..

 

A dangerous game, Rio knew it. But...it was Agatha. Surely, Monday morning everything would be back the way it was. This would be a distant memory, a fever dream more than anything.

 

“Fine..” 

 

Rio’s answer not only caught her by surprise, but the way Agatha’s head snapped up with her eyes bloodshot open? She was the deer in headlights between them both. 

 

She cleared her throat, holding her finger up as each word that escaped her made a statement of their own. Every syllable was loud and clear. 

 

“But this is not a date” 

 

“There will be no friskiness”

 

“And Monday morning when you see me in the hallway- I don’t want to hear a word”

 

“Got it?” Rio asked.

 

Agatha didn’t say anything for a second. She stared and stared some more. Maybe they were close to forty seconds or a minute when the woman finally moved. Agatha’s infamous wicked smile slowly grew wide. Like a snake that crawled along her skin, stretching her cheeks ear to ear with hands up by her sides. 

 

She nodded, each step a smooth stride that brought her closer and closer to the older woman who may or may not have been regretting the decision already. But, it was too late now. Rio signed the deal, secured her ticket in Agatha’s passenger seat. 

 

Sitting in Agatha’s car. With Agatha. Hanging out with Agatha…Oh, what have you done, idiot?

 

Agatha’s shoulder nearly brushed against Rio’s as she stood by her side. She dipped her head down, lips a ghost near her skin. Rio swore she could feel their warmth on her cheek. 

 

The more she thought about it, the feeling was nothing more a wish. Rio wished for her lips to touch every inch of her, to feel how soft they looked, figure out the way they tasted-

 

Oh, this was a bad idea. You hate her. Remember, you fucking hate her. 

 

Rio closed her eyes as Agatha’s breathless laugh sent a chill down her spine. She didn’t offer a moments grace to add a raspy, low, slow, 

 

“Aye, aye- Captain”

 

And as if she was never there, Agatha skipped away while humming along to the music above. Rio took a moment to register the guitar. Her heartbeat was still pounding like a bass drum in her own ears. 

 

But as the guitar tuned in? The familiar intro slithered into her ears and tickled her brain?

 

With Or Without You by U2. One of Rio’s many favorite songs.

 

She pushed off the floor to follow Agatha down to the registers. Rio smirked subtly to herself, watching her hips sway to the smooth tempo. Every step she took added something more to it. The woman would have to wipe the smirk away within a few moments, but for now she’d let it stay. Take advantage of the soft moment to let her eyes linger on the woman she always tried to ignore.  

 

As they walked, the introduction to the song continued to progress. Rio had listened to it so many times throughout her life, but for some reason? The opening guitar riff sounded different. Special, even. Rio wondered if it was just a remastered version. Maybe the crappy speakers that barely worked.

Only when the first lyric broke out in the static sound, Agatha’s voice singing softly to it, 

 

“See the stone set in your eyes..”

 

The memory hit Rio then. No, exploded and shot, kicked and hammered Rio all right there and then. The time Wanda told her life felt different when she met Natasha, her now wife. 

 

“What do you mean different?” Rio snickered. 

 

“Everything!” Wanda beamed with a laugh. “Just, the world was lighter. People sounded lighter. Music sounded..”

 

“Lighter?”

 

“No..” Wanda shook her head, contemplating it before looking up with a soft smile. “Special. Especially the first time we listened to a song together, it…it just felt like the start of something new. A new adventure, something special I-”

 

Wanda snapped her fingers, nearly dropping the red wine glass in her hand from how giddy her mannerisms were. 

 

“I got it!” She exclaimed. “It’ll feel like you were born”

 

Rio chuckled. 

 

“I don’t remember being born, dumbass. None of us do unless you’re like some…crazy memory freak or something, I don’t know” She shrugged.

 

“No, no” Wanda shook her head. “Not like that, I mean…you’ll feel like your life is just starting..”

 

“My life is-”

 

“Oh my god, Rio!” She yelled out. “Stop being so logical, for two seconds. See? This is why the universe doesn’t hear you. You aren’t open to it!”

“By just pointing out the obvious?”

 

Wanda pushed up to her feet, placing the wine down on the coffee table as she paced around the room.

 

“Oh, come on. Where are you go-”

 

The sound of books crashed against the floor. Wanda dropped to her knees, picking through before a-

 

“Aha!” 

 

She jumped back up, rushing over to crash on the couch beside Rio. 

 

“Our highschool yearbo-”

 

Wanda shushed her, bringing a hand up to cover her mouth. Rio snickered, licking her palm which made the other woman cringe and yell how gross she was. During it though, Wanda still made sure to flip through the yearbook until she landed on the sports section. 

 

“Alright, check this out” 

 

“Hm?” 

 

Wanda pointed to their old soccer team. Both shoulder to shoulder in the back row smiling big. 

 

“Yes, we played together,” Rio said. “What does this have to do with-”

 

“The action shots. Look. There’s me running behind you..” Her finger slithered across the page, landing on the goalie. “And that’s-”

 

“Holy fuck, that’s..Natasha!” Rio sat up with a laugh. “When did you figure this shit out?”

 

The woman shrugged.

“Honestly, it’s been such a blur since we started dating-”

 

“Because you live in her bedsheets?”

 

“Butttt!” Wanda spoke over her with a glare. “My point is..trust the universe”


Rio stared, wondering how much her friend had to drink.

 

“So..I need to keep an eye on all my yearbooks? How does this relate to you telling me to cut it out with the realistic shit?”

 

Wanda shook her head, reaching forward to pick her wine back up. 

 

“Because,” She started. “The universe works in ways we don’t understand. It’s not like you and I were small town kids. Natasha was constantly moving as well. What were the chances for her to be right there? To be in the same photo in our yearbook as us?”

 

Wanda took a sip, continuing on right after,

 

“You gotta’ just accept there’s no logic going into destiny, fate, the universe…all of it”

 

“And when it happens, I’ll feel like I’m being pushed out of my mother’s vagina all over again?”

 

Wanda scrunched her nose in disgust as she playfully smacked her shoulder. Rio fell into a fit of laughter. 

 

“Just! Ugh, stop it with the realism and trying to push it” Wanda shrugged, looking over with a warm smile. “When the universe sends you that special someone…you’ll feel it”

 

Rio hummed, taking a swig from her beer. 

 

“Good thing the universe doesn’t send me shit to feel. Just…annoying women like Agatha fuckin’ Harkness” She grumbled. 


Wanda shrugged. 

 

“Who knows, that could be the universe’s person for-”

 

Rio belted out a laugh. 

 

“And on that note, I’m going to grab another beer!” 

 

She pushed up from the couch as Wanda rolled her eyes over her theatrics. 

 

“You’ve met her like once, Rio. The new semester hasn’t even started yet!” She exclaimed. “Who knows, you two could fall in loveeeee!”

 

Rio made gagging noises as she left the room. The woman never knew Wanda mumble a few words under her breath in a mockery voice, 

 

“It’s going to be Agatha…I know these things, idiot..”

 

Agatha placed her items up on the self checkout. She scanned them one by one, carelessly singing under her breath to every lyric. Rio’s plan was to rip her eyes off when Agatha didn’t have her back turned to her. However, with her old conversation with Wanda in her mind, U2 and Agatha singing the lyrics-

 

It felt impossible to look away. Rio tried telling herself this had to be a facade, placebo effect. Maybe her emotions were playing pretend because everything was lining up to Wanda’s words. 

 

The song made her feel like life was beginning for the first time in her life. 

Agatha Harkness, her sworn enemy and most annoying person, was radiating this beautiful light. The world around her felt lighter, happier. 

 

It can’t be her..

 

Agatha cleared her throat, snapping Rio out of her daze to realize she had been holding her hand up to her. She had her lips pulled back, fingers curling back to gesture to herself. 

 

“What uh…wha-”

 

“C’mon, let me scan them”

 

“No?” Rio asked, wondering if Agatha had gone insane. “I- You aren’t-”

 

Agatha rolled her eyes, reaching over to snatch the basket and pint of ice cream from her hand. Just as she did so, their fingers brushed and Wanda’s other words had gone off like alarm whistles in her ears,

 

“And then she touched me..” Wanda recalled. “My whole body just, lit up…it was like being electrocuted but…in the best way possible”

 

Rio felt goosebumps rising up all over her skin. Her eyes began to sting with the sensation of tears threatening her once again. Not because of hatred for the universe, wondering why she wasn’t lucky enough in this lifetime to fall in love, and the being stood up part? Long forgotten.

 

Tears wanted to break free, roll down her cheeks all over again because of the realization there was a burning buzzing through her veins. One that wasn’t painful, but didn’t help her anxiety or anything else going on in her mind at all. 

 

She felt her kneecaps weaken, heart palpitate while her skin vibrated. A piece of her wanted to chalk it up to the sweet offer Agatha was giving her by purchasing her snacks and ice cream. However, Rio knew better than that. 

 

It wasn’t Agatha buying her things..it was-

 

“You’ll know when it’s her..you’ll just feel it and know it, Rio” 

 

Rio watched Agatha place their items in two bags. One was passed to Rio, the other held in her own grip as Agatha ripped the receipt from the printer. 

 

“Alright” Agatha sighed with a smile. “Follow along now, don’t get lost” She winked. 

 

Rio nodded because words didn’t exist anymore. Somehow her feet moved, keeping up with Agatha’s pace as they left the store. The cool air helped settle the vibration through her body, but what it couldn’t help? Rio’s racing thoughts repeating the same thing. 

 

Is it really going to be her? No..it can’t.  

 

Agatha was being nice. Agatha found her crying in the ice cream section, and offered her a shoulder to lean on. She was buying her items out of pity and kindness. Besides, the woman flirts with everyone. Rio wasn’t special. She always knew that.

 

Not to mention, it was clear Rio had hurt her in a way or two. Agatha had never shown that side of her before. Hell, Rio didn’t know that piece of her actually existed. 

 

No. 

 

She told herself as they approached the car. 

 

It’s not her. The universe would not send me my enemy to fall in love with. 

 

“Rio” 

 

The woman jumped, turning on a whim to see Agatha had stopped walking a few steps ago. Rio forced a small laugh, but it was pathetic and didn’t sound like anything. 

 

“Change your mind?”

 

“No! No, uh..” Rio walked back, stammering out the words with a shrug. “Force of habit” She landed on. 

 

Luckily, Agatha bought it and didn’t seem to want to dive into where Rio’s mind had truly been. She gestured to the black Ford explorer. The car Rio knew all too well because it was where her eyes went to in the parking lot each morning. She wasn’t sure when she started making sure Agatha’s car was there, but the habit was one that never died.

 

“Good..” Agatha nodded. “You’d be a chicken shit otherwise. I would’ve had to get you a chicken suit and all” 

 

Rio rolled her eyes, forcing out a monotone, 

 

“Funny” 

 

Agatha smirked as she walked over, brushing against Rio’s back to round the back of the car. She opened the passenger side door, placing her bag on the floor before tossing what Rio assumed was clothes in the backseat. 

 

After a moment or so, the woman leaned back and stepped to the side. Theatrically, she waved her arm with a little bow, 

 

“Your throne awaits”

 

Rio couldn’t help but laugh over that. A genuine one, not a fake or sarcastic response to shut the woman up. 

 

“Such a charmer..” She said. 

 

She hopped into the passenger seat, holding her breath as Agatha shut the door behind her. 

 

Rio took in the interior in the dim light. Only a few wrappers scattered, eyeliner and lip gloss in one of the cupholders caught her eye more than anything. She always looked at the car, the woman who drove or stepped in and out of it. Rio just never thought she’d be sitting in the car. Especially with Agatha in the driver’s seat. 

 

Holy shit. 

 

She was going to be in a car with her. Rio was going to be hanging out with her fucking enemy. Reality was all hitting fast, but abruptly stopped the second the door opened with the chirpy, 

 

“Alrighty” 

 

Agatha sighed as she pulled the car door shut. As she turned the key in the ignition, Rio felt her heart jump again for what felt like the millionth time. Especially as reality had dawned on her where she was, who was beside her and how the entire night had led up to this point. 

 

How did being stood up lead me here? 

I told Wanda Tinder was a bad idea..

 

“Now typically, Vidal. I do have rules for my car” Agatha started. “But..maybe I’ll make you the exception or…you can be my little rule breaker?”

 

Rio felt an ache shoot between her legs over the words Agatha chose. Part of her wondered if Agatha knew exactly what she was doing. Was she feeling everything Rio felt? 

 

From the music, electric touch, everything was lighter and now the familiar thunder of arousal that felt far worse now! 

 

She swallowed the lump in her throat. Rio then forced an annoyed smile as she nodded. No words came out, but luckily Agatha had gotten distracted by trying to find them spoons for their ice cream. 

 

Rio knew she had to break the silence, find her footing and regain the strength she had within her. It was somewhere just…buried beneath the surface, maybe extinct. Wherever it had landed, Rio was determined to find it. The only problem was one repeating thought kept screaming in her mind the loudest,

 

What if it’s been Agatha all along?

 

...Fuck my life...

Late Night Talking, Hemp Plants, and a Whole Lotta’ Denial

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

"If you're feeling down
I just wanna make you happier, baby
Wish I was around
I just wanna make you happier, baby

We've been doing all this late night talking
'Bout anything you want until the morning
Now you're in my life
I can't get you off my mind"


Rio leaned her elbows on the bar, trying to muffle the consistent chatter and music that surrounded her. She didn’t want to be out of bed let alone in public with people at every turn. Especially ones she worked with that expected and damn near required her to be social. 

 

The break up with her ex was still fresh. A wound that barely began to truly heal. It was back in June, right at the end of the last semester everything came crashing down. 

 

She wasn’t happy, plain and simple. It didn’t make sense to her how she could feel the break up cut deep. Wanda tried to explain how it was only reasonable for her to grieve what was. They were together for nearly a year, talking about plans for the future and a possible family. 

 

But, Rio ruined it. Maybe the wound was still there from that. 

 

She hurt someone close to her, someone who saw the good parts when Rio only ever could spot the bad. Wanda was there, she would attempt to tell her it was okay to walk away. Hell, it was only fair. Even if she hurt her, it’d be worse in the long run for Rio to walk into marriage and a family while still feeling empty inside. 

 

Rio was always picky with the people she surrounded herself with. An introvert who did everything to avoid social situations such as the one she was currently trapped in. With that, when she felt someone wasn’t good for her to be around (Even if nothing in particular was wrong with them), she felt the weight of it heavy on her shoulders. In her gut, there was a knot that tightened day by day. The words screaming in her mind how this wasn’t her person to spend eternity with. 

 

“It’ll always be this” 

 

She remembered sobbing, choking the words out while her head rested in Wanda’s lap. Her ex had collected the last of her belongings and it dawned on her then how once again- A woman wasn't the one for Rio to love. She didn’t feel loved or seen in the way her mind and heart desired. 

 

“It’ll happen..there’s some lunatic out there who will put up with you” 

 

Wanda had said those words for years and fuck, Rio was growing tired of hearing them. 

 

Rio glanced at her phone screen, seeing her chat with Wanda still open. The last text she was somewhat ignoring still remained. 

 

Just as Rio was about to pick up her phone, let her thumbs tap away begging for Wanda to save her from this hell hole- 

 

“And over here!” 

 

Lilia’s voice rang in Rio's ears, stopping her from replying to Wanda. 

 

Dammit.

 

Instead subtly dropped her head in defeat, locked the phone and counted down from three before she faced the two behind her. Rio had known Lilia for years, far past her start date as a professor. They went way back into her childhood years when the older woman had lived down the street from her. Safe to say? She knew when Lilia was dragging someone along to meet her.  

 

Rio turned from the bartender to follow it. A warm smile, ready to chat away with whoever Lilia felt she needed to meet and-

 

Holy shit..

 

She didn’t realize how oxygen could be stripped from you so aggressively. Rio had been starstruck by beautiful women countless times before. Gay panic, Wanda said or whatever the hell it was called. Regardless, Rio never felt the sudden rush through her. How everything else around them blurred, only the woman before her was clear as day. 

 

“Isn’t that right?” 

 

Lilia nudged Rio’s arms, snapping her out of the strong daze.

 

“This is Professor Harkness,” She introduced.

 

Lilia had gone on to say something about the English department, but fuck Rio didn't hear her let alone care. She already knew somewhat where the woman would be working, but Rio never knew who it’d be. 

 

She would’ve never guessed either this would be her reaction. 

 

LIlia went on to joke about how Rio was a witch with nature. A force to be reckoned with when the landscapers on campus were in her vision. Typically, Rio would be flattered and acknowledge such comments with wits of her own humor.

 

However, she was distracted and seemingly- So was the new professor. 

 

The older woman wasn’t blind and Rio knew that, but she chose to ignore that. Without a doubt, Lilia was seeing the way the two stared each other down. Both in their own world, exploring each other’s eyes, never breaking apart. 

 

“Well..” Lilia drew the word out, taking a step back. “I see uh, I’m needed over by Professor Kale. We both know how she gets with..”

 

Did Lilia complete her excuse to walk away? Rio wasn’t sure. All she knew was Harkness now stood alone before her. A small smile was growing on her lips, eyes let go to roam up and down Rio’s body which suddenly felt small- Even if she was a slight inch taller than the woman. 

 

“Vidal,” 

 

Her voice was something extraordinary. A sound Rio had never heard, a blessing to be introduced to. The way her name rolled off her tongue, it glided with ease and ran smoothly in the space between them. 

 

“The meaning of life?” 

 

As if her voice alone wasn’t enough- Her knowledge stepped out with power. A force that took Rio aback. No one ever guessed or cared to know the meaning of her last name. Hell, it never seemed anyone was interested in the five letter word. 

 

“Is uh..” Rio straightened her back, taking a sip of her drink before tilting her beer forward. “Studying words, a hobby of yours?” 

 

The woman smirked, a small shrug followed with a small,

 

“Only to impress beautiful women like yourself” 

 

Before Rio was able to digest the flirtatious comment- The woman’s hand was extended and she introduced herself with confidence that radiated power throughout the room, maybe the entire city to every continent. 

 

“Agatha Harkness” 

 

Rio nodded, lifting her hand that was trembling as adrenaline coursed through her entire body. Their first touch was electric- A vibration that trembled Rio down to her core through the floorboards beneath her. 

 

“Rio Vidal” 

 

She managed to introduce herself within a few seconds, but the way Agatha was smirking- Did she see the fluster through her warm cheeks? How Rio was becoming a mess under her stare?

 

“Rio” 

 

Agatha echoed with a soft smile, slowly nodding before asking, 

 

“So…you're a green witch?” 

 

Wha- Oh, shit, Lilia…course…Rio thought to herself. 

 

The older woman had called her The Green Witch since she took over Lilia’s garden back in middle school. What started as a science project turned into something spectacular. Lilia would always laugh, saying how she (Who had years of gardening experience) never managed to make the flowers and plants blossom the way Rio could.

From that moment on, Rio earned the nickname that she secretly adored. 

 

She cleared her throat, adjusting her shirt as she stood a bit taller. 

 

“Um..” Rio shrugged. “Less a green witch, more The Green Witch” 

 

Agatha puffed out a small laugh, shaking her head and Rio thought she stuck the landing. Maybe this conversation, meeting, party- It wasn’t bad after all. The only downside was she’d have to tell Wanda how she was right, but..that was the last thing on her mind. 

 

“Ego filled thing, aren't you?” Agatha asked. “I’m sure I’ve seen better”

 

Oh..

 

Rio wasn’t sure if Agatha meant for her comment to come off harsh. Did she realize the attitude that covered each word? How she sounded absolutely disgusted with her? 

 

Or…was Rio just thinking too much into it?

 

Most likely, it was the second, but..Rio’s insecurities weren’t always good remaining on the surface. Especially fresh off a break up and from a woman who was dominating the air around them. 

 

She narrowed her eyes, watching the way Agatha looked so smug and something in her stomach kicked. A switch was flipped, the sparks flew but not in the way it did before. 

 

“What makes you so sure?” Rio questioned. 

 

Agatha shrugged, taking another sip of her drink. 

 

“I know these things”

 

“So..you know how much of an asshole you sound like right now?” 

 

That seemed to eliminate the smug look on her face. Instead, it was replaced with shock and Rio was able to take the step above- Finally. 

 

“This usually work for you?” Rio gestured between them. “Just…insulting someone off the bat?” 

 

Agatha clicked her tongue, head tilting to the side as she tapped her fingers against the wine glass. 

 

“What? Are you not like other girls?” The woman asked. “Don’t like to be brought back down to earth a little bit?”

 

Rio laughed, rolling her eyes as she shook her head. 

 

“You don’t even know who I am to be making the call if I need to be brought back down to earth to begin with” She argued. 

 

“I know ‘em when I see ‘em” Agatha shrugged. 

 

“Wow,” Rio said. “I could say the same about you being an asshole right about now-”

“You could or will?” Agatha smirked. 

 

Rio paused before she scoffed, pushing her back off the bar to storm past the woman. She let their shoulders punch against one another, muttering under her breath, 

 

“Fuck off, Harkness..”

 

Little did Rio know that’d become her new mantra for years to come...

 

 

“Rules for your car?”

 

Rio wasn’t sure how she thought of the words, but she sure as shit wasn’t going to question it. Somehow, she’d managed to pull herself together…well, and least somewhat. 

 

Between the adrenaline coursing through her veins as if the emotion was her blood. How Wanda’s cursed words bounced around her brain, preaching the universe held its own magical ways. And Agatha’s fucking little flirts suddenly feeling as if she’d push Rio off the edge of glory. 


She always flirted with her. Annoyingly, that was. Why was Rio feeling different all of the sudden? Sure, she always felt a bit flustered and even turned on against her own wishes at times. But this was another level, an intense feeling that only grew with everyone. 

 

“Mhm” Agatha hummed. 

 

The older woman scoffed, suffocating her true feelings the best she could. 

 

“You're joking..” Rio muttered. 

 

Agatha snickered. 

 

“Far from it” 

 

The younger woman continued to rummage through her center console for plastic spoons. Both had forgotten to grab some for their ice cream, too distracted by one another to remember. But, Agatha had insisted she had them somewhere. Rio assumed she must’ve stored them from different drive thru’s and such. 

 

Which felt very Agatha. Rio wasn’t surprised to see her car was complete and total chaos. However, how the fuck did a hot mess have rules for her car?

 

“I’d give you a rundown, but your tears are excusing you from it” Agatha waved her hand towards her as if she tossed the rules away. 

 

Rio scoffed. 

 

“What? Do they excuse me from signing a waiver as well?” She asked with her tone covered in sarcasm. 

 

Agatha snapped shut the center console in defeat. She dropped her head, shaking it subtly before silently hissing a small, 

 

“Shoot!” 

 

The woman then looked up, meeting Rio’s eyes as she added on a slow,

 

“I knew I forgot something at home..” She sighed. “I’ll email you the documents tonight. Just sign them and send it back to me” 

 

Easily, Agatha had dragged Rio in another moment where she wondered if the joke was serious or not. Though the confusion didn’t last long as that sickening wide grin crept up slowly. The one that confirmed Agatha was in fact joking and there was no car rule contract. 

 

Course..

 

This is what drove Rio mad at times. Agatha was so good at lying, joking, pulling one over you without any energy needed. Rio swore Agatha didn’t know how to go twenty four hours (Let alone a fucking second) without making some kind of joke out of a situation. 

 

“Ha. Ha” Rio’s voice was monotone as she rolled her eyes. “I knew there was no way you had rules for your car-”

 

“Now that,” Agatha pointed. “That is actually truthful”

 

Before Rio was able to reply- Agatha leaned over to pull down the glove box. Which would be fine, but it was the position she had put Rio in. One moment Agatha was on her own side of the car. The next her shoulder nearly brushed against Rio’s lap, hair just below Rio’s chin, sparking that same electric sensation as before. 

 

This time the feeling was stronger, more powerful as their close proximity was in a compact space. 

 

The lavender with a hint of vanilla conditioner wavered through the air, sneaking up into Rio’s nose. She had to hold her breath to keep her composure. Plus, Agatha was laced through the conditioner. The woman carried something of her own. A smell Rio couldn’t figure out, but could only describe it as, 

 

Agatha. 

 

“Ah, here we go!” Agatha exclaimed, snapping Rio out of her shock. 

 

The woman leaned back as if she was never over Rio’s lap, untouched by any emotions that Rio was overwhelmed with. Part of Rio fell into jealousy, but also embarrassed as fuck because it was clearly, just her. Agatha wasn’t phased, she wasn’t feeling the chaos of emotions Rio had been since she agreed to join her in the car. 

 

Agatha held up the spoon wrapped in plastic, a smile of achievement matching it. Rio muttered a small thank you, taking it from her to rip the plastic off. She balled it up, placing it in her lap before taking the seal off her ice cream. 

 

The older woman’s mind was still swimming in Agatha’s orbit. The warmth in the air over her lap grew cold with the abrupt absence. She hadn’t even spent more than fifteen seconds and Rio was drowning as if Agatha trapped her for hours. 

 

Go back to the rules. 

Get out of your head with this. 

Focus.

 

“Nice try,” Rio said, clearing her throat right after. “For a woman who barely holds standards and rules for a classroom, there’s no possible way you-”

 

“Rule number one!” Agatha cut off, holding a finger in the air. “Thou shall not complain about my driving”

 

Oh my god..

 

“Well, I’m not going anywhere with you. So..that rule is pointless right now” Rio argued. 

 

Agatha rolled her eyes, but continued on as if Rio hadn’t said anything at all.

 

“Number two,” She continued. “Thou shall not criticize the car’s possessions. She likes stuff, clothes and random objects one wouldn’t think to carry, but end up needing anyway! Hence the spoons” She tilted her head with a smirk at the end. 

 

Rio peeled the lid off her ice cream, leaning forward to flip it upside and rest on the dashboard. She sat back, crossing a leg over the other when she realized-

 

“Wait..” She said, rolling her head over slowly to see Agatha busy with her own wrapper. “ She as in who? You or-”

 

“ She as in the vehicle you are sitting in right this very moment”

 

Yep. That’s what I thought. She really is insane. 

 

“You gave your car a gender?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha gasped, smacking a hand over her heart as she shook her head before looking at her with disgust.

 

“Professor Vidal, she is more than just a gender!” She exclaimed. “She has a name!”

 

“Oh!” Rio laughed, digging into her ice cream because she needed some kind of vice to continue putting up with this. “And what would that name be, hm?”

 

She hummed, slipping the spoon past her lips to let the frozen treat greet her tongue.

 

“I don’t think you deserve the honors to know” Agatha huffed, returning her attention to peel the lid off her ice cream. 

 

Rio snickered, shaking her head. 

 

“Because there is no name”

 

“Yes, there is,” Agatha argued.

 

“No, there isn’t” Rio countered. 

 

“Yes. There. Is” 

 

“If there was, you’d give up the name”

 

“I just said you don’t get to know-”

 

“Which is something one would say when it’s a bullshit lie!” 

 

“Ugh, fine!” Agatha groaned. “It’s Violet. Named after one of my favorite shades of purple” 

 

Rio paused, watching as Agatha took a small dig in her own ice cream. No humor or smirk to prove otherwise. She was serious. Her car had a gender, rules, and was named after not just her favorite color- But, one of many shades of it. 

 

“You’re so lame” She shook her head. 

 

“Oh, as if you aren’t yourself!” Agatha exclaimed. 

 

“My car doesn’t have a name” Rio rolled her eyes. “So, I don’t think I’m the lame one here,” She added. 

 

Agatha worked to finish her bite of ice cream, waving her spoon in the air as she swallowed before replying, 

 

“No, but it is commonly known on campus how Professor Green Witch views all her plants as her children” Agatha argued. “Don’t sit here and tell me you did not baby talk that little cactus”

 

Rio’s cheeks began to burn. She took another bite of the ice cream while hiding her face. Agatha snorted, crumbling up the plastic with a small,

 

“Mhm! That’s what I thought”

 

Rio shook her head.

 

“Whatever, continue on with Violet’s rules” She said. 

 

Rio caught a glimpse of Agatha’s ice cream container. The Ben and Jerry’s chocolate chip design dim in the parking lot’s light. Before Agatha was able to carry on, Rio realized then? She had more ammunition to shoot at her for who was the lame one. 

 

“Wait, wait” Rio laughed, pointing over with a strong, “You insult my rocky road, think I am the lame one, but get fucking chocolate chip?!” 

 

The younger woman looked down at her ice cream, shrugging with a tiny smile. No teasing, taunting, none of it lined up behind that grin. The dim parking lot lights casting soft rays through the windshield offered Rio access to see the subtle pink shading Agatha’s cheeks. She looked away as if she caught on to Rio catching it, hiding herself as she scooped up her own bite of ice cream. 

 

“It’s a classic,” She pointed out. 

 

Rio snickered. 

 

“It’s boring and lame”

 

“Like you?” Agatha rolled her head over, a tiny grin while popping the spoon between her lips. 

 

And suddenly Rio was jealous of a spoon getting to feel and taste something that she desired. 

 

No. No. That’s not what this is, shut up. 

 

Rio looked away in a hurry, desperate to derail the conversation back to where they previously were. Agatha seemed to feel the same as she took the lead to do so. 

 

“And number three,” She said, drawing out the silence as if it were anticipation. “Thou shall not control the music when it is not their car”

 

Right after she stated the final rule (Or what Rio assumed was the last one), Agatha reached for her phone and unlocked the screen. She navigated with a few taps, passing it over for Rio to see the Spotify home screen staring up at her.

 

“Aka, the rule I am eliminating for thee” Agatha smiled. 

 

Rio stared at the phone, feeling her heart kick up once again. Not because of the Spotify app, but it was the way Agatha had said she was eliminating the rule for her. 

 

The woman was offering for Rio to choose the music. Her voice telling her that was soft, delicate, brought warmth into Rio’s heart and- 

 

No.

 

This is out of pity. 

 

No. 

 

Agatha found her crying in the ice cream section- This. Is. Out. Of. Pity.

 

No. 

 

She flirts with everyone and nothing about this is special. 

 

I am not special to her. 

I’m her enemy. 

I hate her. 

She knows it. 

 

The older woman cleared her throat, tightening up her shoulders before letting them drop with a low, 

 

“In exchange for..?” 

 

Agatha looked confused for a moment, wondering what she meant by that. She shook her head, lips pursed in a tiny pout as she replied, 

 

“No exchanges,” Agatha said. “Nor a trick,” She added. “Just a trial”

 

“A trial?” 

 

Rio scoffed, looking back up at Agatha who had her eyes locked on her as if she was the most interesting thing in the world. Fuck , that didn’t help anything about this. 

 

“Of what?” Rio managed to choke out. 

 

Agatha smirked as if she expected Rio to ask more questions. 

 

“If you have immaculate or pathetic music taste” Agatha nudged her phone at her. “Come on, now. Chop chop”

 

Rio hesitated before she caved and took the phone out of Agatha’s hand. She placed the pint of ice cream in her lap, both hands free to let her thumbs search for an artist. 

 

The amount of pressure that weighed on her to choose something good was heavy. She thought about what song would make Agatha want to talk to her more, but at the same time? The annoyance, resentment, and hatred still ran deep. Denial wasn’t a river in Egypt to her quite yet. Rio was holding on to what she knew for three years and pissing or annoying Agatha was her plan. 

 

Well…so she thought, anyway because unbeknownst to Rio? She was already going to choose a song Agatha would like. Even if she wasn’t thinking about doing so. Her heart was ruling over her mind. The secret villain in her pulling all the strings. 

 

She typed in the words, clicking the song before passing the phone back to Agatha who was leaning forward to turn the volume up. The intro began and the title on her dashboard came to life. Rio picked up her ice cream, taking a frantic nervous bite as she awaited Agatha’s response. 

 

A puff of air left Agatha with a tiny scoff when she read the words, 

 

“I Still Haven’t Found What I’m Looking For

                            U2”

 

“More U2, huh?” Agatha asked.

 

“I always leave this store listening to this kind of music,” Rio shrugged. 

 

“Not a bad thing” Agatha hummed, bobbing her head to the soft beat. 

 

They let the music fill the silence for a bit. Agatha had grabbed her phone, opening to the song’s radio so the one song wouldn’t play on repeat. But, they’d still have the same vibe as it. 

 

Though, when the song was closing in to the end- Agatha broke the unspoken minutes between them to break the glass and ask- 

 

“So..are we going to talk about the tears in the ice cream aisle or what?” 


Rio snapped her head over, eyes wide as she shook her head frantically. 

 

“What? No. You said we’d listen to music. That was it”

 

“I say a lot of things,” Agatha snickered. “Besides, I feel like that plan was eliminated when one was sobbing at ice cream. Who cries over ice cream?”

Rio stared wide, suddenly feeling her stomach and feeling sick because she could not talk to Agatha about this. It was one thing agreeing to hang out with her, but another to admit to the woman who already gave her hell left and right her Tinder date stood her up. And Rio just knew Agatha would never let that go. 

 

“It’s..no,” Rio said before chuckling over the idea of even saying anything about it. “I can not talk to you about this”

 

“Is it work related?” Agatha questioned. 

 

Rio shook her head. 

 

“No..”

 

Agatha hummed. 

 

“Well, that’s a surprise”

 

“What’s that supposed to mean?” 

 

“Isn’t everything in your life related to the university?”

 

Rio rolled her eyes because great , this topic. Wanda, Lilia, even Jennifer had jumped on her from time to time over it. 

 

“You should live life outside of work”

“Work doesn’t need to be what you live and breathe”

“Won’t you regret spending all your life on work one day?”  

 

“I don’t think it’s a bad thing, Rio” 

 

Wait, what?

 

“If anything, it’s admirable” 

 

Rio fell into a deeper pit of disbelief because Agatha Harkness, the woman who teased and taunted her every second they were near one another. She always seemed to like poking fun, digging under her skin to push every button that would aggravate her nerves. 

 

How the hell was she not making fun of Rio for such a thing? She insulted her teaching methods left and right. Rio remembered well the first argument the two had ever gotten into. It was during a get together with the others for drinks. Agatha and Rio sat across from one another at the table. She couldn’t remember exactly what sparked it, but she knew Agatha lit the flames between them. 

 

“Well, I like to make sure students don’t fall asleep in my class. Professor Vidal, you should take notes from that. Don’t you think?”

 

“Oh shit..” Alice mumbled behind her drink. 

 

Rio snapped her head up, eyes narrow as her lips slowly curled into a smirk. One that was vicious, venom on her tongue ready to poison the air between them. 

 

Agatha Harkness was already someone she couldn’t stand to be around. Her voice was loud, annoying and way too much for her low energy to handle. And now she was going after her teaching methods? 

 

“Is that so?” Rio asked. “Are your students even there to learn? Or do they just want an excuse to have a party mid day?”

 

Agatha snorted through her little laugh. The one that made Rio’s stomach flip and irritated her both at once. 

 

“My students like learning because I make it lively and fun. Yours on the other hand, well” She shrugged, taking a pause so she could sip her wine before continuing. “We all have heard you’d much rather be kind to your plants over stu-”

 

“Oh!” Rio laughed. “Really? Because I hear students that don’t even give a shit about the material they’d learn in your class. You’re just eye candy to them”

 

“You think I’m eye candy then?” Agatha smirked like the devil, threatening to strip Rio’s soul right then and there. 

 

This bitch...Rio muttered in her mind. 

 

The woman scoffed before she slammed down the rest of her wine in one swallow, pulling her wallet out to leave cash before abruptly standing up. 

 

“Guys..”

“Rio, sit down”

“C’mon” 

 

The others piled words over the other, but Rio was having none of it. 

 

“No, no” Rio put her hands up. “It’s fine. At least I can sleep knowing I’m teaching my students something over just letting them stare at my ass and party all semester”

 

Rio never stayed to hear what Agatha had to say. Instead, she stormed off without looking back. She rarely agreed to go out for drinks or attend dinners with them after that. Which part of her was thankful Agatha ever did that. Even if it was wine induced or God knows what. It gave her an excuse to stay home and that’s all she could really ask for. 

 

“I mean, come on. Remember our professors? How many genuinely craved teaching others? You’re beyond passionate about fucking plants too. I mean, hell, I didn’t know one could view them as humans. Do they actually have feelings?”

 

Rio felt her cheeks flame red, looking down and wondering all over again when Agatha’s switch had flipped. She wasn’t insulting her teaching style, but this time admiring it. 

 

This is all out of pity, has to be..

 

But hey, if Agatha wanted to ask about plants? Rio could never deny that topic. She could be speaking to the most evil human on earth and if they asked her something related to nature, she’d be more than happy to discuss. 

 

“I mean..” Rio shrugged. “Realistically? No. They don’t” 

 

Without thinking, Rio found herself perking up in her seat as her worlds began to spill uncontrollably. No filter, no breaks, just an unstoppable train that ran off on it’s own. 

 

“However, I’d like to think since they are living creatures- Yes, creatures, they are that to me. They need water and oxygen just as we do to stay alive and they grow and lose life just as we do and so maybe, yeah, I’d like to think they could potentially have feelings and emotions. Maybe we just aren’t meant to figure that out…but, I always uh..”

 

Rio turned her head over to see Agatha with a gawking stare her way. Movements frozen, lips sealed shut as they slowly were pulled back between her teeth in what Rio would guess was an attempt to not burst out laughing. 

 

Embarrassment flooded her when realization dawned on her. Agatha was joking just like always. She didn’t care or want to know. Rio just couldn’t shut the fuck up and not make a fool of herself over a stupid fixation. Since a kid, this had hjaoppened. No one ever wanted to actually know how insane she was when it came to her plants.  

 

Especially the woman she couldn’t stand. 

 

“You were…joking, right-”

 

Agatha snickered, confirming Rio’s doom was approaching sooner than expected. 

 

“Yeah, kinda’ but…” She shrugged. “Not going to argue that theory of yours. You could be right, who knows?”

 

Rio sunk into the seat, suddenly not hungry and regretting every bite she took. Agathha must’ve seen it written all over her the way her words rushed out.  

 

“But, nice to hear this isn’t work related and you do have a life outside of the university” She said. 

 

Rio didn’t say anything. She was too busy debating jumping out of the car, abandon the snacks Agatha had purchased for her. Maybe even skipping town without a bag packed or a look behind her.  

 

“I won’t tell a single soul what is said in this car” Agatha said. “Scouts honor” She held up her hand. 

 

Rio chewed on the inside of her cheek, debating if it was worth even admitting to. 

 

I mean…it’d make her forget how much of a loser I sounded like over stupid fucking plants..

 

No, no. What are you thinking? 

 

Don’t do it. 

 

She’ll never let it go more than sobbing in the fucking store. 

 

Do not-

 

“Tonight was- I’m supposed to be at a..dinner. Woman from fucking Tinder” 

 

Andddd, you’re resigning and leaving the country. 

 

Agatha snorted and Rio’s heart flipped upside down, ready to drop beneath the pavement below them. 

 

“If you’re going to laugh at me, I swear Ag-”

 

“You don’t think you’re the only one that’s happened to, right?” Agatha asked, almost condescendingly. 

 

Bitch. 

 

“Oh, totally” Rio rolled her eyes. “Jesus, is this another insult? Are you calling me self centered right now? I’m not saying this as some woe is me shit or-”

 

“No, I’m saying it because I was stood up tonight as well. Jesus..” 

 

Agatha’s words created a silence between them. Just the soft background noise of Time After Time by Cyndi Lauper through the car speakers. Rio looked closely, making sure this wasn’t one of Agatha’s tricks. If it was, it’d be a brutal one. That’s for sure. But as Agatha focused on stabbing her spoon in the ice cream, shaking her head while muttering,

 

“Why else do you think I’m in the fucking ice cream section begging the co worker who hates me the most to sit in my car with me?”

 

She’s serious..

 

“You’re lying..” Rio mumbled. 

 

It was a last effort attempt to figure out this was just another cruel joke of her’s. Agatha just scoffed, shrugging as she spoke, 

 

“If I am, hit me with one of those plant vase thingys of yours because that is the most embarrassing lie ever” She huffed. 

 

“Vase thingys?” Rio asked. 

 

“Yeah they look heavy…breakable” Agatha said. “Regardless, I was supposed to be on a date myself. Not sure what happened. She cancelled like an hour after being late”

 

“Oh..”

 

“Mhm”

 

“The univer-”

 

Shut the fuck up, Wanda..

 

Rio thought the words to herself when the memory was about to replay in her mind. How timing and all things related to the universe wasn’t supposed to make sense. It was unpredictable and this felt like something related to all of that. 

 

What were the chances of them both being stood up on the same night?

How could they possibly decide to grab ice cream at the same store, same night, same time?

 

All of it screamed the universe had a hand in this game and Rio wasn’t sure what to do with that quite yet. If anything, it terrified the shit out of her because Agatha was her enemy. She was the one woman she fought and bickered, avoided for three years now. Why would the universe choose Agatha of all women that existed?

 

“What’s your favorite plant?” 

 

Rio looked up when Agatha broke the silence, taking a second to register the question. 

 

“What?” 

 

“A plant? Oh sorry, creature” Agatha smiled a bit as she took another bite, asking again this time with a mouthful of the frozen treat. “Which is your favorite?”

 

“You…you really want to discuss… plants?” 

 

Agatha didn’t bother answering the question. Instead answering her own question since Rio didn’t bother to. 

 

“Mine would be the azalea flowers, purple specifically. My mother hated them with a passion and they always grew in our garden against her will. Witchcraft shit, really” She snorted. “I’ve adored them since-”

 

“You adore something your mother hated?” 

 

A weight dropped upon them. The energy in the car shifted into something tense. A heavier energy Rio wasn’t quite able to narrow down the reason for, but..she could tell Agatha became very uncomfortable. It was a new look she wore. Something Rio had never seen in the three years of knowing her. 

 

Whatever it was, Rio felt the swift urge to redirect the subject back to her own answer. Rio slowly smirked herself before rasping a low, 

 

“Hemp flower..” 

 

Agatha froze before she snapped her head up, eyebrows furrowed as her lips curled. 

 

“What?” She asked.

 

“My favorite. It’s-”

 

“Weed?!” 

 

Agatha cut her off and Rio could only laugh how her voice slightly broke in between. A high pitch crack that sent a tingle down Rio’s spine. 

 

“Oh, don’t gasp as if you think it’s the worst thing in this world” Rio shook her head with a wide grin, proud to have caught the woman off guard. 

 

“No, no, not the worst thing- Far from it! Just..” 

 

Agatha laughed with her hand up, readjusting in her seat to face her completely. She put the ice cream in the cupholder, hands together as she grinned like a mad woman. The reaction was adorable even if Rio didn’t want to admit it. 

 

Truthfully as time went by, the more words and longer they spent together- Rio was finding she didn't want to acknowledge or face a lot of things. 

 

“Jesus, Vidal. You are so, way, wayyyy far too uptight to smoke let alone grow fuckin’ weed! There’s no way you-”

 

Rio took a bite of her ice cream as Agatha was bursting with excitement at the new found information she had on her. She slowly slipped the spoon out of her mouth- A tiny grin formed while rolling her head back over to Agatha.

 

“Who do you think Lilia’s dealer is?” She asked. 

 

The younger woman gasped as her jaw dropped. She slowly let out a laugh that turned into multiple tiny snorts. One after the other, trying to catch her breath while choking out the words, 

 

“No way!”

 

“Way” Rio confirmed with a small nod. 

 

Agatha sat back, eyes glimmering as she took in the new found information about her enemy. The professor who always seemed so angry, stern, distant and cold to ever feel warm beside her. Now here she sat in Agatha’s passenger seat, slowly pulling back the curtain to reveal who Professor Vidal truly was outside of the classroom. 

 

When she saw the stoic, brave, confident woman a wreck in front of ice cream, of course Agatha felt her heart ache a bit. But as the minutes went by, more words were said between them- She couldn’t help but feel thankful for those tears. Who knew they’d lead to a moment like so?

 

“Well,” Agatha smirked. “Your shit is pretty good. I have to give you that”

 

“What do you mean?” Rio questioned. 

 

“Lilia offered me to smoke with her one time. Little did I know the devil’s lettuce I was inhaling was crafted by Professor Green Witch herself” 

 

Rio scoffed, looking back at her ice cream in hopes Agatha wouldn’t see how her cheeks burned over the little nickname and compliment. Instead, she focused on the name for the marijuana that Agatha used over the other that made her heart flip.

 

“Devil’s lettuce” She muttered. 

 

“It’s a fun name for it!” Agatha exclaimed, shaking her head with a swift, “Should’ve found you crying in the ice cream section years ago if it meant learning this about such a now shockingly grumpy professor”

 

“You’re never letting the ice cream section thing go, are you?”

 

“Smoke with me and find out, professor” 

 

She’s going to be the death of me..

 

The next hour flew by them like a gust of wind. They talked way more than Rio thought could ever be possible. Sure, when they met years ago there was energy between them. But, it had gone sour so quick. Barely reached the top of the mountain before tumbling and spiraling back down. 

 

Agatha told her the latest gossip with her students. Both figured out they had a toxic relationship duo in either class. Rio had the boyfriend, Agatha had the girlfriend. The two laughed as they mocked and rolled their eyes over the students' theatrics with their dramatic fights. Which led into conversations about other students, but both unspokenly skipped over discussing teaching methods. 

 

Rio didn’t know if it was intentional on Agatha’s end to do so, but it surely was on her own. After being stood up, the complex emotions that exhausted her by the second- Rio didn’t want to find herself in an argument with Agatha. 

 

And what she wouldn’t admit to herself quite yet? She didn’t want to stop what was going on between them. 

 

It wasn’t the constant sarcasm and bantering. Neither found a reason to bicker either. Sure, a few insults were tossed back and forth. But it was different compared to their usual. The insults were filled with laughter, feigned annoyance, all of the above. 

 

Rio couldn’t understand what was going on. All she could chalk it up to was both of them took pity on each other. They had been stood up, finding themselves on a late night trip for junk food to eat their feelings. Agatha had found Rio crying while Rio witnessed Agatha plead for her to hang out. 

They were taking pity on one another and nothing more. That had to be it. 

 

Eventually as the clock teetered towards an hour after midnight, Rio had called it and said she had to get home. Agatha seemed disappointed, but the look didn't last long. Rio assumed it was exhaustion that made her see the delusional reaction, not thinking more on it. 

 

“Thanks uh,” Rio stepped out of the car, looking back up when her feet planted on the concrete. “For this..” She added. 

 

Agatha smiled, head tilted back against the seat and oh hell- Rio swore the look made her feel tipsy as if she downed a bottle of jack. Suddenly her mind was swimming in a flood of confusion and wonder, trying to decipher if the tears and tiredness had won or if it was genuinely just Agatha. 

 

The woman looked so content. A lazy smile that Rio never had access to before. She was used to vicious smirks, exaggerated grins everytime she managed to make Rio storm off. Not whatever this was, but…what Rio knew? She loved and hated it more than words can say. 


And what didn’t help the feeling she already had found herself drowning in?

 

“That woman is a moron, Rio” 

 

She said it so effortlessly as if the thought had been on her mind since Rio told her. The lazy smile had faded, but not in a bad way. Instead she subtly frowned. One that told Rio her words were sincere and again, Rio didn’t know what to do with it. 

 

“Is she?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha pulled her lips back while humming a small, 

 

“Mhm” 

 

But, Rio barely heard it. She was far too aware of how her eyes were watching her every move. How Agatha was burning lasers into her while Rio was quick to busy herself. She grabbed her phone, wallet, making sure she had everything and Agatha was watching her every single move.

 

“She missed out..” 

 

Rio froze for a second before jolting back up. She scanned over her belongings, making sure she had everything. There was a passing thought to leave something so she had an excuse to venture back here. 

 

She didn’t leave anything behind (Well…physically, emotionally and mentally was up for debate). 

 

“Yeah..” Rio nodded, clearing her throat a second after. “Also uh, thanks for..buying this” 

 

She held the bag of junk food Agatha had bought her in the air with her words. Agatha perked up in her seat right as she said it, reaching forward to find her keys.  

 

“Just a pity gift,” Agatha shrugged with a tiny grin. “I’ll see you on Monday and no worries, this never happened” 

 

She tilted her head back up and fucking winked . Rio genuinely was losing her mind and hoped Agatha wasn’t able to see any piece of it. 

 

“Take it easy on yourself, Vidal” 

 

Rio nodded. 

 

“You too..”

 

Rio went to shut the door, feeling the vehicle vibrate as Agatha started up the engine. But like a force of nature that held a will of its own, she spun around to add a quick,

 

“Your ghost was stupid too” She rushed. 

 

Agatha was in the middle of buckling herself in when she shot her head up, looking like a deer in headlights. It was clear how she didn’t expect it and Rio took some joy out of that. 

 

“You’re annoying, don’t get me wrong,” Rio quickly added. “Like, insufferable and everything, but uh…yeah” She shrugged with a shake of her head. 

 

Slowly Agatha grinned that lazy smile all over again. Her cheeks burned red under the dim light and for a moment Rio thought to herself,

 

Is she feeling everything just the same?

 

“Ghost..” Agatha echoed the word. “Nice little name for her”

 

Rio smirked. 

 

“Sometimes I’m good”

 

“Eh” Agatha shrugged. “Night, Vidal”

 

The woman scoffed, shaking her head while she tried to look as annoyed as possible. But the three familiar words she spoke had a smile forced through them against her will. 

 

“Fuck off, Harkness” 

 

Rio had said the words, slamming the door shut without a second to spare. Through the window, she felt her heart grow warm when she heard Agatha belt out a warm laugh. A cackle that her little snort trickled through.

 

She spun around, pulling her lips down to bite on while trying terribly to hide the wide grin that wanted to shine bright. Rio walked through the parking lot to her car, too busy in her head to notice how Agatha waited till she was safe in her own car. When she slithered in the drivers side, that’s when she heard the two beeps. Her eyes shot up, seeing Agatha’s hand flying in the air, but not with a normal wave. 

 

“Oh..that bitch” Rio chuckled. 

 

Agatha had waved her middle finger in the air and Rio could vision so clearly that familiar antagonizing grin that went with it. She shook her head, buckling her seatbelt and started the engine up. 


Her plan originally was to go home, bury herself in bedsheets with a tub of ice cream. And out of nowhere, that had flipped like a coin. What was heads became tails and Rio knew which side she was fond of most, but would she say it to herself? No. That’d be ridiculous. 

Instead, her eyes fell to her phone in the cup holder and like a threat?

 

Check her Instagram..

 

“What?” Rio asked out loud as if someone else said the words. 

 

Why would she look at Agatha’s Instagram? That made zero sense! There was no reason to, Rio did not care, Monday was just around the corner and they’d be back to usual. Neither would acknowledge this night ever happened. Agatha would undoubtedly give her a reason to remember why she hated her to begin with. 

 

“No..” Rio muttered to herself with a laugh. 

 

She clicked her seatbelt, pressed her foot on the brake before shifting the car into drive. However, she never moved to the gas pedal. Instead her body was frozen as if checking Agatha’s Instagram would unlock her, free her from the chains she had found herself in. 

 

Gotta’ be kidding me..

 

Rio aggressively shifted back into park, snatching her phone up as if it was her opponent she was determined to defeat. 

 

A few seconds of stalking couldn’t hurt, right? Besides, it’s not like Agatha would know she ever looked. Rio made sure to first run a quick search off of Google, confirming Instagram wouldn’t tell Agatha she had checked her profile. 

 

She held in a deep breath while navigating through Jennifer’s followers, landing on Agatha’s account. 

 

Motherhark. 

 

Right, how could Rio forget that username? She had only looked once a few years ago, but didn’t bother to really pay attention. Agatha had requested to follow her and Rio denied it. That was that. 

 

And now here she was, clicking into her profile to see only the few posts that were up. Five, to be exact. That came as a shock to Rio, truthfully. She heard the few others including Agatha talking about reels and memes, god knows what else. 

 

Rio was never one to be on social media much. She much preferred being outside, working in her garden or taking her dog out on hikes through different nature trails. She had adopted a stray that wandered into her yard a year prior. A black pitbull lab Rio had named as Nicky. She wasn’t sure why, but simply went with the feeling in her heart it was the right name. 


Safe to say, social media was rarely on Rio’s radar. 

 

She pulled her lips back, clicking on the first post and just like that-

 

Fuck. 

 

 

Rio brought the back of her hand to her lips, pressing and biting down gently on her knuckles. This couldn’t be happening to her. A simple fucking selfie of Agatha and she felt as if her body was being set on fire. 

 

Her eyes scanned the woman’s jaw line from left to right. Rio’s eyes had always wandered there, but how her head was tilted back made it more present. She fought of thinking about how it’d feel to trace her fingertips along the bone, suck, press down soft bites and kisses and-

 

I need to stop. 

 

But, she couldn’t stop. Not when her eyes trailed down her neck. The veins that popped out like a threat. The same thoughts rushed through her mind. She wondered how her skin would feel against her tongue, how Agatha looked with dark hickies as if Rio was some owner desperate to mark her property. 

 

She isn’t yours to even mark. What the hell are you thinking?

 

The glasses were a rare sight. Agatha only wore them once in a while. Rio swore only Agatha knew how to make big frames work. Lilia tried, but everyone laughed and said she looked like an old kook with them. The older woman shunned them all for a week after that, but the glasses never made a return. 

 

And the worst of all? Her lips. Agatha Harkness’s fucking lips that moved with every annoying word she spoke. So vibrant, filled with life, almost begging for Rio to attack them with her own. And her eyes daring into Rio’s as if she was posting that photo solely for her. 

 

This was torture. Pure hell that Rio was putting herself through. 

 

She shook her head, letting her thumb scroll to the next post that luckily eased the lust boiling within her. Instead, her teeth lifted off her knuckles as a tiny puff of air filled with humor pushed between her lips. 

 

Rio remembered the Halloween party vividly. Funny enough, it was Wanda who dragged her along as if she worked in the university herself. Rio had a plus one for the event, Wanda was adamant it was to be her. Which worked out because Rio’s co workers adored the red head and it took attention off of her. 

 

She remembered briefly seeing Agatha in the outfit. A rock star straight out of the seventies. Rio didn’t allow herself to linger long, slipping through the door, leaving an Irish goodbye to head home. She hated parties, but hated more how good Agatha looked in that outfit. 

 

But, Rio couldn’t hate the party. Not when Wanda had the time of her life or the bartender ended up giving her a few free shots. Lou Miller who Australian, tall with an attitude Rio instantly felt comfortable with. They even ended up exchanging numbers and Rio ended up becoming good friends with her. 

 

So no, Rio could not hate or dwell on that party. Especially seeing Lilia being in a photo. She always hated and avoided those. 

 

Rio continued on to the next photo and her heart swelled even larger. A tiny amused grin became warm. So soft she would nearly melt at the touch. 

 

As much as Agatha gave that boy hell, acted as if he was an annoying nuisance- Everyone knew Agatha borderline adopted him like he was her own. If anything, William (Billy was becoming his name more these days or just Kaplan) seemed to be the light that shined in Agatha’s life. Not to say she was a miserable grump before he was hired, but she certainly became different in a good way when he did. 

It wasn’t surprising she took time over the summer to help him become a better driver. Rio began to wonder what other adventures they went on and if the side she saw of Agatha tonight was a snippet into the soft natured person she could be. Through the rough exterior filled with sarcasm and insults, a wicked grin that threatened to annoy you till the end of time- 

Rio felt as if she was wrong. Was Agatha more than just that? And was Rio really starting to crave figuring that out more? 

No. She wasn’t, she couldn’t. And yet, she still scrolled.

Right, the nice Agatha was announced and introduced to them all. Rio remembered that night very well. Not just because she didn’t want to be there, but it was when Agatha and her first met. What started off as intriguing and flirtatious became the start of a feud that would last years between them. 


She clenched her jaw, the smile fading as the reminder punched her in the gut. Agatha wasn’t going to continue to treat her like she did just before. It’d go back to the place they started. A feud between them, arguments and snarky comments. Rio would return to hating her even if she lusted after her as well. 

 

Shouldn’t Rio be happy this was a reminder for that? Rio should take a breath and become relaxed over it.

 

So…why did she feel slightly disappointed?

 

Whatever, one more post. 

 

 

Rio snickered, the smile returning as she softly laughed to herself. 

“The fuck are you wearing, Harkness?” She muttered to herself. 

She wore a baggy flannel, shorts and boots with a ridiculously large cowboy hat to top it off. Agatha looked utterly ridiculous and Rio tried to figure out why the hell she was dressed like that. 

Maybe it was Covid brain that had gotten to her. Lockdown did drive everyone insane. Not Rio, she wished the lockdown lasted forever. Being paid to stay at home? Being told to stay away from people? How could Rio ever hate that? It was her dream life and she missed it terribly at times. 

However, Agatha seemingly was losing her mind during it or…was this just Agatha? Was she silly this way? Did she love being the most confusing woman ever? 

And better yet, why did Rio care so fucking much? 

Just..go home. She told herself. 

Rio exited the app, locking her phone after making sure her Spotify kept playing music. Once she was situated, she put the car in drive, pressing on the gas to take off out of the parking lot. 

It wouldn’t be until later on, possibly her next visit, it’d occur to her how the store in the rearview was tainted. Anytime she’d step inside, her mind would soar straight to Agatha singing a few steps away. She’d look at the ice cream pints, wait for the woman’s commentary on every flavor. Plus insult the ones Rio chose for herself. 

Grocery shopping would never be the same.

Parking lots would suddenly feel too empty. 

Being alone in the car would become quieter than before. 

 

Overall, Rio’s life would never be the same. It already wasn’t the moment her eyes locked with Agatha’s. She thought about the woman way more than she realized, but now? Oh. It was different. Everything had changed and Rio hadn’t entirely realized it. 

 

She turned the volume dial up for her music to play a bit louder. A song she had listened to every now and then, mostly when it came on shuffle in one of her mega playlists on Spotify came into clarity. Use Somebody, King of Leon. 

 

“You know that I could use somebody…someone like you”

 

Rio mumbled the lyrics to herself, barely registering the meaning or how it happened to be the first song that played off shuffle. If she did realize it, she’d be too busy denying and cursing the universe for trying to say Agatha was never meant to be her enemy.

 

Agatha Harkness was the woman Rio couldn’t stand. She hated her, despised and avoided her at all costs. 

 

You are not going to fall for the fucking enemy, Rio.. She said to herself. 

 

Rio shook her head as she mumbled to the song, trying to shake off the memory playing in her mind as she drove down the road. 

 

“Remember when we were kids? Like, when we wished for something every shooting star that passed?” Wanda asked. 

 

Wanda and her were laying in the backyard after a day of moving furniture and boxes nonstop. Rio had just moved into her new home. A tiny cottage tucked away from society. A bit of a farther drive from the university, but it was worth it. 

 

Rio slowly exhaled the smoke, passing the joint over to Wanda who happily took it from her. 

 

“Yeah. When you used to wish for longer hair” Rio snickered.


Wanda chuckled. 

 

“It worked!” 

 

“No, you just didn’t get it cut for three years”

 

“It still worked,” Wanda shrugged, taking in a small inhale. As she held it in her lungs, she swiftly added. “You wished for the same thing on repeat and never told me what it was, you know?”

 

Rio scoffed. 

 

“Duh. Then it’d never come true”

 

Wanda laughed as she choked on the smoke through her exhale. 

 

“Oh, come on! We were kids, is it still the same wish or something?”

 

“Ugh,” Rio groaned. “Kind of. Maybe. I don’t know”

 

“Tell me” Wanda pushed, holding the joint in the air from her. “Or you aren’t getting this back”

 

Rio rolled her eyes, muttering under her breath how annoying the woman was. But she simply started to hum a tune as if she had all the time in the world to hate. 

 

“Fineeee,” Rio drew out the word in an annoyed tone. “Maybe I’ve wished…or used to- Yeah, used to. I dont’ waste time wishing anymore-”

 

“You so do”

 

“Do not”

 

“Do to”

 

“Do you want to know or not?!” Rio asked. 

 

Wanda surrendered, gesturing for her to continue on as she took another hit. 

 

“I guess..I don’t know, it’s stupid” Rio muttered, sitting up to run her hands through her hair. She held the strands back, tugging at her roots as she looked down. “I just..I love being alone, but-”

 

“Don’t want to die alone?” Wanda asked. 

 

Rio puffed out a bit of air with a tiny shrug. 

 

“Just feel like I make enemies all the time, you know?”

 

Wanda pushed up on her elbows, holding the joint in front of her to take. Like it was her reward for opening up on what her truest wish was. 

 

“Hey, who knows..” Wanda shrugged. “Maybe you’re meant to experience the enemies to lovers trope”

 

Rio was taking a hit when she broke out in a strong laugh. 

 

“What?!” Wanda exclaimed. “It could be true!” 

 

“Doubtful..” Rio said, turning her head over her shoulder with a low, “Those tropes are a headache. A disaster waiting to happen”

 

“And yet, sometimes the worst turns for the best,” Wanda said. 

 

The redhead pushed herself up, their shoulders pressed together as she reached over to steal the joint back. 

 

“I wouldn’t rule it out,” She advised. “The world works in mysterious ways”

 

“You and the universe bullshit..” Rio muttered.

“Enemies to lovers, Rio. That’s your destiny. I can feel it in my bones”

 

Rio laughed. 

 

“You’re stoned. All you’re feeling is an order of Five Guys or Taco Bell right now”

 

“Ooo,” Wanda’s eyes lit up with a lazy grin filled with an appetite. “Both sound so good” 

 

“Of course they do..” Rio snickered. 

 

She held tight on the steering wheel, remembering the “enemies to lovers” trope conversation as if it was right before sitting with Agatha. But, Rio still took in a strong breath while chanting in her mind how ridiculous that was. Agatha wasn’t the enemy she was meant to be with. Not when it’d be three years of pure torture having to endure her. 

 

As she drove, her mind started to drift back into the music. Focus on each song and ignore the lyrics' meanings. Everything would be fine. Monday would come along, they’d go back to ignoring and hating one another. This night would be a blip, a fever dream, something that never happened. 

 

But, what Rio wouldn’t figure out until the next day? Her thumb had slipped on one of Agatha’s posts. When she rushed to exit the app, she brushed over the heart icon and liked Agatha’s post all the way from Covid. Rio was so frantic and quick to drive off, desperate to ignore her interest in getting to know Agatha more. 

 

The first Instagram post Agatha had ever posted was from years ago and Rio fucking liked it. Agatha would get the notification, figure out Rio borderline stalked her right after they parted. Rio had signed her death certificate and hadn’t even known it yet. 

 

She would be too busy getting in the house, rushing to bed to see the notification that appeared on her screen that night. A habit of her’s was to clear her notifications, ignoring everything until the next day. Rio would be greeted with her death certificate in the morning. She’d open her phone to check all emails, messages, any notifications she might’ve missed. 

 

The notification would be the most life threatening, stomach dropping, heart racing one she’d ever lay eyes on.. 

 

“Motherhark has requested to follow you”
