7 Things, a Rage Room, and Regrets

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

"It's not possible for me not to care
And now we're standing in the rain
But nothing's ever gonna change until you hear
My dear

 

The seven things I hate about you
The seven things I hate about you
Oh, you"



The sunrise slithered through the bedroom curtains, casting little golden streaks across the room. Rio’s eyes slowly flickered open to the light. Matched with Nicky sniffing her up and down, pawing at her leg with the unspoken request, 

 

“I’d like to go outside, Mother” 

 

She slowly turned over, ruffling the hair on his head with a lazy smile. 

 

“Morning, bud. How’d you slee-” 

 

A yawn cut her greeting off, stretching her limbs and felt the bed shift as he launched off of it. His paws skidded down the hall, racing for the back door before she could finish her question. 

 

Rio pushed herself out of bed, always thankful for the boy who entered her life. He was the reason she was able to move on her worst days. Even through her darkest moments, his energy and life radiated through her. 

 

She rubbed her eye while stepping down the hall, into the small kitchen to find him tapping at the glass screen as if Rio had kept him hostage for days. She scoffed with a little laugh.

 

“Jesus, dude. Ever heard of Stockholm Syndrome? Why not fall in love with your captor instead?” She joked, unlocking and pushing the door open for him to fly out of. “Run along now” 

 

With fire under his paws, he rushed out and ran into the yard. Rio had gotten a fence around her backyard the second he came into her life. It was a game changer to say the least. She was able to leave the door open for whenever he wanted to come back in, letting her drift off to start her day. 

 

That was the thing about Rio, a curse she joked was set upon her. No matter the hour, if her eyes opened and body moved- She became restless. It’d be three in the morning and she’d end up packing her lunch for the day, taking a shower and getting dressed. Slumber never came easy to her. She wondered at times what it was like to have a full night’s rest. 

Rio clicked the coffee maker on as she walked by, heading into the bathroom for her morning routine. 

 

The night before felt like a fever dream as it slowly trickled back to her. The memory of Agatha was fuzzy, how she found her in the ice cream aisle crying her eyes out. Then invited her to sit and eat their feelings together. It all felt surreal, foreign, as if she made it all up to cope with the idea of hating her. 

 

How the fuck would that make sense? Rio muttered in her mind. 

 

What didn’t make sense to her either? Possibly more than just that? Agatha being stood up as well. Rio couldn’t wrap her head around the idea of that happening. Not a chance. That had to have been a lie because- 

 

Who would give up a chance to be with someone that hot?

 

With the toothbrush in her mouth brushing off her back molars- Rio froze. 

 

Don’t think that. Rio told herself. 

 

Rio brushed her teeth harder to the point her gums subtly felt a pinch of pain. She was desperate to shake that thought away because, no! Rio hated Agatha. A simple two hour hang out session wouldn’t change that!

 

Sure, yes, okay- Agatha was hot. That thought had always been there no matter how much Rio hated it. 

 

However, the more the memories of the night before came into clarity..

 

Oh my god. 

 

Rio spit out the toothpaste, rinsing her brush off while tipping back the water to swish. Her cheeks stretched just as wide as her lungs, mind racing as her heart sunk to the floor beneath her feet as she realized,

 

She’s hot. Like. Hot, hot. 

 

Agatha’s grin she gave before they parted ways burned in her mind. She felt the same energy seethe through her veins. How her lips looked so delicate, soft, warm to the touch. Her eyes were lazy with tiredness from the day and night’s events. Even through her exhaustion, she smiled at Rio like the woman was the sun peaking out of a cloudy day. 

 

Fuck. 

 

Rio didn’t know what to do. Should she put in her resignation? That’d be a good start. Maybe she’d spend the morning apartment searching and give her place up to someone else. Honestly, she didn’t care if her savings would be drained by the end of it. 

 

Escaping Agatha Harkness was the only answer possible. 


Truthfully, Rio knew she’d never grow close to doing such a thing. The woman adored her job, students, the people she worked with (Minus a certain someone). She loved her home, the town she lived in, how her two closest friends lived five minutes away. 

 

So, as peaceful as an escape sounded- Rio wouldn’t dare make that move. 

 

Besides, she wasn’t going to let Agatha win. If either of them were the one to jump ship, skip town- It should be her. 

 

I was here first..

 

Rio checked to make sure her coffee mug was being filled. Sometimes it took a few smacks against the machine to get it working. One day, she’d buy a new one. She just never had a reason to do so. 

 

It wasn’t that she was cheap. Rio had made a decent living and savings for herself over the years. More so the reason stemmed from her special talent. Wanda had nicknamed her years ago,

 

“Particular Procrastinator” 

 

Rio remembered hearing Natasha break down laughing, agreeing with her partner up and down. She looked over confused, asking for an explanation. 

 

“You procrastinate only on certain things in particular” Wanda shrugged. 

 

“Everything besides work, more like” Natasha added. 

 

Rio scoffed. 

 

“Bullshi-”

 

“You literally kept your mattress till your back was so sore you barely were able to stand up!” Wanda laughed. 

 

“Your laptop had a crack in the screen for years,” Natasha added. 

 

“Oh! Don’t forget her microwave barely cooked anything! Took ages to heat up a soft pretzel”

 

“And when she-”

 

“Okay!” Rio yelled. “Point taken. Loud and clear, but..” She shrugged. “At least all my work is done before an hour till the deadline” 

 

Natasha and Wanda both booed, sticking their tongue out while the other flipped her off. Rio snickered, sinking back in the couch with victory- Even if she was a procrastinator. 

 

The steaming liquid poured into her coffee after she smacked it on the side a few times. Rio smiled to herself with a small,

 

“See? You’re still working” She mumbled. 

 

Glancing outside to check on Nicky who was rolling around in the grass, Rio smiled softly. The warm sunny patch that Rio imagined felt good on his back would leave a mess all over his fur, but she didn’t mind. She always chose his happiness over frustrating messes. 

 

She then moved to find her phone on the counter, plugged into its charger. Rio scoffed, thinking how it was impressive she even remembered to charge it. Late nights or not, it was a bad habit to let her phone die twenty four seven. 

 

Rio expected texts from Wanda and Natasha in their group chat, pestering her on the date and asking how it went. She already dreaded having to admit to being stood up, but hey- It’d get her an excuse to not let them make dating profiles or set her up on blind dates in the near future. 

 

When the screen lit up, a few notifications were listed off. Random reels being sent to her, email articles that she didn’t care for, and as she expected- The group chat eagerly awaiting her updates. She didn’t have it in her to talk, not yet. Later in the day that’d be a hill she had to climb over. 


The coffee maker beeped, signalling her cup was ready for her. She whistled a soft tune, sitting her phone down to stroll over. A tiny bit of milk, a small bit of sugar, she brought the burning liquid to her lips. Typically, she waited for it to cool off, but…after last night’s events? The day ahead? She didn’t care how it’d burn. 

 

“Shit!” 

 

She hissed, squeezing her eyes shut as the seering sting ran over her tongue and down her throat. Rio shook her head, collecting herself before picking her phone back up. 

 

Emails would be the first app to open, making sure she didn’t miss anything important. 

 

Next, Facebook to check her memories. Lilia loved tagging her in things, but today was empty. Another sigh of relief she wouldn’t have to be social more than her two friends. 

 

Instead of ignoring the reels on Instagram, Rio decided to check them out. That’d settle Wanda’s harassing just a tiny bit. Enough to save her mentality and well being somewha-

 

Holy fuck. 

 

Rio clicked the notifications when she saw the little icon that signalled someone requested to follow her. It’d be a bot or someone from high school who would be way too eager to reconnect. But no, her worst nightmare sat in the waiting room to be accepted. 


As if the words were in all capitals, bold, daring, life threatening and ready to kill Rio on the spot-

 

“Motherhark has requested to follow you”

 

Rio dropped her phone on the counter. Somehow remembering to gently place her mug down instead of letting it crash all over the floor. Her feet took two steps back, her palm pressed tight against her lips. 

 

What the fuck?

How did she-

There’s no way she knows I looked. 

SHE CAN NOT KNOW I LOOKED, RIGHT?!

 

She felt sick to her stomach. The tiny sip of the bitter liquid swirling, ready to shoot back up as if it’d been rejected. 

 

This couldn’t be real, no. Rio must’ve had to be still dreaming. That was the only explanation for this! She Googled it, made sure Agatha would have no idea she checked and stalked her profile like some creep.

 

Wait..

 

A thought popped into her mind, the only answer that settled her fear- 

 

She thought about my Instagram..

Yes..yes! That’s it! 

 

She wanted to stalk me just as I did with her- No. Nothing weird about us having the same thought. No. Nope. She’s the creep, not me. 

 

Rio reached back out to pick her phone up, thumb hesitating over the reject button. Though as if she had a magnet under her skin, her phone was a fridge or a locker- She felt the screen press against her thumb and just like that-

 

Agatha Harkness had followed and gained access to Rio Vidal’s Instagram.

 

This is fine. Everything is fine. 

 

No one would notice or say anything. Agatha would most likely be a nuisance and send her even more reels than Wanda did. That was that. She didn’t even have to follow her back. The interaction could be a one way street- 

 

You had to accept the follow though…so, is it still only one sided or-

 

“No..” Rio muttered. 


She started to laugh, putting the phone down to pace across the kitchen tiles, sipping from the burning liquid that suddenly felt numb. Rio felt her thoughts screaming in circles around her. As if they were a bunch of little demons having a world war of their own. 

 

The first side was trapped in a deep state of disbelief, screaming out the words,

 

This can’t be real. 

What the hell did I just do? 

Is..this is all a nightmare..it has to be, oh my g-

 

The other side was hard at work, rationalizing and trying to alleviate the situation. Rio was 

 

No! No, it’s fine.

She followed me. 

She invited me to hang out. 

This is all Agatha, not me. 

 

In the back of her mind was a soundtrack. A lingering tune that was an orchestra, enhancing and egging on the dramatic battle between her thoughts. She’d barely been awake for twenty minutes and the day felt long, never ending. 

 

Block her.

Fix this before it’s too-

 

Rio had rushed back to her phone, hands shaking as she swiped the screen open. Her thumb tapped onto Agatha’s profile only to have the notification pop up above.

 

Late..

 

Is this how being murdered feels? 

Jesus, don’t be that dramatic. 

 

“Fuck my life..” Rio muttered. 

 

Whatever. This didn’t matter. Agatha texting her didn’t have to mean anything and furthermore, Rio was not required to offer a reply. Agatha wasn’t entitled to her attention. She was lucky enough Rio had (For whatever reason) accepted the follow request. 

 

Why did she follow me?

 

The question started to itch her brain, scratching as it begged to dig up the answer. The delusional side of her wanted to believe Agatha simply craved being annoying. Maybe she got the wrong idea after the night before. It was all pure hope to save herself from the possible, biggest, complete and total embarrassing move she’d ever pull. 

 

“Like what you see..”

 

Those words slowly demolished her hope brick by brick, piece after piece. The deep tug in the pit of her stomach pulled tighter. 

I made sure to not like anything..didn’t I?

 

Reviewing each post again felt dooming, but at the same time inevitable. Her fingers trembled as she tapped the screen, bringing her back to the familiar profile. No new posts, the same sight as the night before remained. She held her breath, clicking the selfie that choked her the first time and-

 

Fuck. 

 

The reaction remained the same. A chilling sense of desire, her taste buds tingling with the need to feel Agatha’s skin- Taste her lips and-

 

“No, no, no. Stop it” Rio muttered to herself.

 

Her thumb aggressively swiped, flying down the posts until she saw the red heart bright as can be. 

 

“Like what you see..”

 

The four words echoed into the void of her soul. She felt her pulse beating through her, a screeching ring in her ears and Rio swore she could hear the blood flowing through her veins come to a stop. The birds outside, trees swaying in the breeze, all of it was silenced. 

 

Who knew a red heart could feel so life threatening?

 

Rio Vidal had liked one of Agatha Harkness’s Instagram posts. Not a post from a year ago. Not two, not three, not four, but- FIVE YEARS ago. 

 

‘March 27th 2020’ to be exact. 

 

The Covid post where Agatha stood in a cowboy hat and boots. When Rio had smiled to herself with a shake of her head, wondering what on earth she was wearing. She liked it. Her thumb either slipped or she was drunk on exhaustion to register the action. 

 

“Oh..my..god” She muttered to herself. 

 

She had to fix this. Even if it meant talking to the woman who was bound to give her hell till the end of time. Rio figured Agatha would berate her to the grave over liking her first ever Instagram post. 

 

The first one. Fucking first..COULD’VE LIKED THE RECENT ONE AT LEAST!

 

Rio screamed at herself silently, racing to open the chat she originally planned on ignoring. It wasn’t a surprise either Agatha hadn’t taken a millisecond to reply.

 

Rio scoffed. 

 

At least one thing from this was worth it. Rio was remembering exactly why she couldn’t stand Agatha Harkness. Even if she seemed kind, gentle, warm and sympathetic- She was ready to use Rio’s most (Well, now second compared to the Instagram shit) embarrassing moment of her life against her.  

 

And yet? 

 

Oh no. 

 

She gripped her phone, staring wide at the messages while a new thought joined the party in her mind. 

 

I can not actually like her teasing me..

There’s no fucking way. 

No, I-

 

Another message from Agatha popped up, bringing her back from the edge of panic. The cliff edge Rio was preparing to jump off of left abandoned. 

 

Argue her. Be mean. Show her you don’t care. 

 

Rio nodded to herself, letting her thumbs work their magic. Well, she hoped that would be the case. 

 

She had to block her. That was the only way to end this nightmare Rio was convinced she’d have to wake up from at some point. 

 

However, Rio continued to sip from her coffee, staring at Agatha’s profile dumbfounded by the new found thoughts in her mind. How part of her fucking liked Agatha teasing her. She couldn’t resist staring at the latest post. That stupid selfie that made Rio crave and envision horrible, disgusting, perverted things. 

 

Why are you letting this happen?

 

Rio had zoned out to the point she didn’t notice how much time had passed until Agatha messaged her again, snapping the woman out of the daze she had fallen into. 

 

 

“Oh my godddd!” 

 

She groaned, tilting her head back as she squeezed her eyes shut. Just when she thought the situation couldn’t possibly get worse, it does. Even more so how Agatha was waiting on the other side. 

 

Rio wondered if she was still in bed, leaning on her kitchen counter just as she was, on the couch or-

 

Stop thinking about what she’s doing while texting you, creep. She told herself. 

 

Rio muttered some curse words of annoyance under her breath. Once again, she decided replying was her only option. 

 

It is my only option. Not because I want to talk to her more…or anything. 

 

(Anddd, that was a lie!)

 

Good. Don’t give her another answer. 

 

Rio smiled to herself, relief and pride hitting her when Agatha didn’t reply within a few seconds. Though, it was short lived and Rio should have been prepared for that. 

 

The notification appeared on her screen with words that didn’t just annoy her, but also made her heart skip a few beats. She felt the way her breathing staggered because of it. 

 

 

She can’t be serious. 

 

 

Oh, fuck this bitch. 

 

Of course, why should Rio feel any amount or speck of surprise Agatha was using blackmail to her advantage?

 

Bet she’s included in the definition of that word. 

Ignore her, don’t give her the satisfaction of it. 

 

As if Agatha was hearing her thoughts from afar, reading her mind like a book- The next text popped up just before Rio was able to exit the chat. 

 

 

We’d be a delicious combo- Oh no. No. No. NOOOO!

 

Rio shook her head, eyes shut tight. She smacked her thigh a few times as if it was her coffee maker, shaking it to drain all the liquid out. 

 

From a nightmare to a night terror, Rio was convinced she was trapped in one. Or, maybe she died and this was hell. Whatever her new reality was, it felt damning. Alarms were blaring in her mind, she swore she could see the red lights spinning for her to evacuate. 

 

I can not fall for her. I can’t.

 

This is lust. Nothing more than just lust. 

 

She opened her eyes, rereading the few messages back and forth. A bell rang in her ears. One that belonged to a high striker in an amusement park. Her realization was the sledgehammer, pounding downwards and hitting the thought above. 

 

I have to confirm this is nothing. 

 

What? You can not possibly be debating hanging out with her again! 

 

It’s the only way!

 

No, no. There’s other options and-

 

I have to know this is just…nothing. No crush. No deeper feelings. Just. Fucking. Lust. 

 

You can’t!

 

 

She locked her phone, placing it back on the counter while her eyes flickered up to the imaginary camera in front of her. She felt like Jim from The Office, giving his well known deadpan stare that said,

 

You’ve got to be kidding me.

 

Rio ran both her hands over her face, palms digging into her skin while fingers traced through the bed tangled hair. She slowly felt the weight of seeing Agatha on her again. Hating her was becoming more difficult by the second. How the fuck was this going to make that any easier?

 

The argument in her head had settled down, sizzling to a simple question Rio would be asking herself all day and night,

 

What is wrong with me?

 

 

Rio sat in the parking lot, trapped in her car she hoped wouldn’t open. Maybe she’d get lucky somehow and all four doors would be sealed shut. She’d simply shrug, mouth an ‘Oh well’ before zooming off into oblivion. 

 

Her escape thought was hopeless for the first ten minutes, but she felt hopes lift up as every second went by- It’d be possible. 

 

They ended up agreeing on a time for six PM. Rio being the punctual person she was- She had been ten minutes early to be on time. Agatha on the other hand unsurprisingly was now ten minutes late. 

 

Two opposite ends of the clock, Rio could only hope that was another reason to hate her. 

 

She took a sigh, head tilted back while her eyes stared through the car's sunroof. The sky was cloudy, a grey doom that matched the energy this hang out was sure to be. The night before was two souls longing for emotional support. They had stumbled into one another and that was that. 

 

With the aftermath of being stood up fading away piece by piece, Rio told herself this would be different. They’d argue, banter, possibly even hit one another with baseball bats instead of the objects designated for such actions.

 

Or, maybe they’d never get the chance to do so since Agatha still hadn’t shown up. 

 

Come on, Harkness..

 

Wait..what? 

 

Rio flipped her head down, eyes wide as she stared out the windshield. Had she truly wished in some form for Agatha to show up?  

 

Only because I want to confirm this is nothing. 

 

Yeah…that’s it. 

 

(No. It wasn’t)

 

She didn’t have a chance to dwell on the thought much longer. Her eyes drifted over to the familiar vehicle parking in the row ahead of her. Just a few spots away to her left. Rio sighed of relief and despair, undoing her seatbelt in hopes the car doors would magically be glued shut. 

 

Of course, the door opened right up. A gate swinging wide, almost flying off the hinges with excitement for her to step on through. 

 

Rio shut the door with a bit of flair behind her. A flick of her wrist that said, fuck you to the car for working. She shook her head, muttering a few curse words incoherently while pressing the lock button. After making sure she had her wallet and phone, Rio spun around and-

 

“Fuck me..” Rio muttered. 

 

Not that way (Yes that way).

 

Agatha stepped out of her car with a chocolate donut held in her mouth . 

 

Suddenly I want to be a don- Don’t even finish that thought, idiot.

 

The denim black jacket draped over a familiar blue flannel she’d wear on Friday’s. Her hair was pulled back, barely held by the loose hair tie. 

 

She looked so… normal? No. That wasn’t the word, but Rio was too dumbfounded to think of the correct one. 

 

Agatha Harkness was always polished. Her personality and teaching methods were not, but the outfits and signature design screamed a different side. 

 

From the pantsuits, trousers and button ups that always had a few undone. Even with the familiar flannel, Agatha was able to make it fancy. 

 

Even if she looked more laidback than usual, Rio still felt her outfit wasn’t enough. The blue sweater that almost slipped off her left shoulder. Only part of her hair pulled back, still messy from her slumber. She wore her black jeans and a knock off brand to the Converse high tops, a memory hitting her as she glanced down at the pair. 

 

“I’m not a cheapskate, Wanda. I just don’t give a fuck when I can get the same ones for fifteen dollars” 

 

“God. You’re so boring” 

 

The memory of their interaction from a few weeks ago made her stomach flip. Would Agatha care about them? Was she someone who admired name brands over knock offs from Walmart?

 

Fuck it. If she cares, I can hate her more. 

 

Rio cleared her throat, striding through the parking lot to meet her. Agatha was busy chewing away, rummaging through what Rio assumed was her purse. She leaned in the passenger seat where Rio had sat hours prior. 


Was Agatha thinking about that?

Did she already fill the vacancy as if Rio never existed?

And why the fuck did Rio care to know?

 

The woman leaned back up, slamming the door shut while glancing to her left. 

 

Rio stood with her arms crossed, holding them tight against her as if she could restrain the complicated feelings and never let them escape. But as Agatha’s smile grew wide, those blue eyes somehow shining with no sun in sight- 

 

Oh. Why did I agree to this?

 

“‘Ere she is!” 

 

The woman’s words were muffled with the remaining crumbs of the donut in her mouth. Rio should cringe, find it repulsive, but instead-

 

Ha. Cute- No. 

 

“Took ‘ou long ‘nough” Agatha added.

 

Rio scoffed, not bothering to point out how Agatha was late. She had a feeling that would be useless to dwell on. 

 

“Sorry, I don’t speak donut ?” She asked. 

 

Instead of chuckling over the tiny joke or returning a humorous one of her own. Agatha’s jittery movements froze. Even her chewing came to a stop for a few seconds before they continued. Slow chomp after chomp, what looked like a rough swallow to finish it off. 

 

She slowly smirked, arms folded against her own chest to mirror Rio’s stance. 

 

“Oh?” 

 

Her voice was pitched in a teasing tone. Rio felt her heart skip a beat, anticipating words that were sure to damn her into a state of embarrassment.  

 

“The remainder of that donut was in my mouth before you got over here” 

 

She pointed out. It didn’t take a rocket scientist to figure out where Agatha was going with this. Rio dug her nails into her palms, lips pulled back while she waited for the final bullet to hit her chest.  

 

“Were you watching me, my little stalker?” 

 

Shit. 

 

Fix this. Fix this. FIX IT!

 

Rio shifted on her feet from one side to the other. A weak scoff while her eyes rolled to avoid the narrowing eyes on her. 

 

“In your dreams” 

 

Agatha took a second before she snickered. Eyes of her own rolled back and Rio cursed herself for watching. 

 

Her every move is getting to me. God. I need to get laid so this stops. 

 

(Rio could sleep with every woman on the planet and Agatha would still make her crumble. Of course, she wouldn’t admit to that)

 

“Well then,” Agatha held her hand up to the building, tossing her back an annoying grin. “Shall we?” 

 

No. 

 

“I guess,” Rio shrugged. 

 

Agatha took the lead for them both, giving Rio access to watch her from behind all over again. How her hips swayed as if she knew to give the woman a show. Her head held up, confidence and power radiating for miles around her. 

 

Rio hated it. She hated her. And she hated even more how Agatha opened the door, stepped aside with her arm swaying inward, 

 

“After you, professor” 

 

She rolled her eyes, muttering a low,

 

“Thanks” 

 

Agatha brushed her shoulder against Rio’s while walking ahead again. Rio wondered if it was on purpose, but forced her attention elsewhere. 

 

The room was empty besides them and the worker at the counter. She scanned the posters of people destroying things with malicious grins. The sounds of music from down the hall with bottles of glass breaking echoed, but were covered up by Agatha’s voice.

 

“Yeah, just the two uh..” She said, looking back. 

 

Instead of asking her, Agatha let her eyes roam Rio from head to toe. Almost as if the move was intentional, looking to make the woman shiver under her stare. Rio swore too it burned red lasers and left marks beneath her clothes.

 

“I’d say large”

 

Did she just pick my size for me? 


And why is that kind of…hot?

 

The worker nodded, disappearing into the back room to grab what Rio assumed was the jumpsuits of protection people were wearing in the photos. 

 

“Think I’m fat?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha smirked. 

 

“Tall,” She said, leaning an elbow on the counter with her palm propping her chin up. “I learned the hard way their suits run short” 

 

Rio rolled her eyes. 

 

“I’m not that tall. You’re like what? An inch shorter than me?”

 

“When I’m not wearing heels that make you look tiny, mhm” She hummed. 

 

Before Rio was able to visualize the memory of her heels that threatened to shatter the university floors, the worker popped back up with neon green jumpsuits in his hands. 

 

“Alright,” He smiled. “Gloves and jumpsuits here. You guys are in room seven. Right down the hall you’ll see our helmet selection and-”

 

Agatha smacked the counter twice with a wink. 

 

“Thanks kid,” She said. “I’ve got it from here” 

 

He stammered a few times before giving up and sitting back down. Agatha whistled as she handed Rio her gear, leading them to the hallway of different rooms. 

 

Rio scoffed, but not over the ugly color of the gear in her hands. 

 

“You didn’t have to cut the poor guy off” 

 

Maybe she did. That helps me hate her. 

 

Agatha sighed. 

 

“I’m excited,” She shrugged, smirking over her shoulder with a raspy, “Punish me” 

 

Nevermind. She should not have done that. 

 

The number seven was spray painted on the door like a jail cell. Rio wasn’t sure if she was a fan of how it looked either. The door was heavy, slid open and shut like they were two inmates stepping into their doom. 

 

I swear. If we get stuck, I’m killing myself…and her. 

 

Rio followed Agatha by pulling on the jumpsuit over her clothes. It was pretty simple, but the zipper on the back decided to put up a fight. Her eyes flickered over to Agatha who was grabbing their helmets, seeing she had managed to secure the back with ease.

 

How experienced is she with this shit?

 

She grumbled a few insults at the zipper under her breath, wrists growing sore from trying to pull it up. Though what made her wish the pain would’ve stayed at the forefront? The familiar electric shock trembled through her body. 

 

“Your shades of green are nicer, that’s for sure”

 

Agatha spoke so casually as she pushed Rio’s fingers away. As if this was their normal and she helped Rio get dressed a million times before. Rio heard the zipper fly up with ease, Agatha stepping back as swiftly as she appeared. 

 

Jesus. 

 

Rio raised an eyebrow. 

 

“What uh…what do you mean?” 

 

She managed to break through the aftermath of her shock to ask. 

 

Agatha picked up the gloves, pulling on the left before her right. That smirk Rio swore hadn’t left at all stayed present. She then shrugged as if her words were obvious. 

 

“Your wardrobe is ninety-nine percent dark green” Agatha pointed out. 

 

“Oh” Rio replied. 

 

Oh? That’s it?

 

Agatha grabbed the motorcycle helmet, flipping it upside down to hold the straps on each side. Her smirk finally faded away and Rio felt as if she could take a breath. That was until she realized what it had been swapped for. 

 

She felt smacked by the memory of the night before, remembering every piece of it well,

Agatha smiled, head tilted back against the seat and oh hell- Rio swore the look made her feel tipsy as if she downed a bottle of jack. The woman looked so content. A lazy smile that Rio never had access to before. She was used to vicious smirks, exaggerated grins everytime she managed to make Rio storm off. 

Not whatever this was, but…what Rio knew? She loved and hated it more than words can say. 

“Not a bad thing” Agatha assured.

 

That smile is worse than any other look she owns. Rio swore. 

 

The woman forced her attention to the gloves followed by the helmet, determined to focus into rage over whatever the hell Agatha gave her. Butterflies? Flustered? Disgust?

 

Yep. The third one. Has to be. 

 

And as if the universe had it out for her. Almost as if it was desperate and fed off of her embarrassment more and more, 

 

“Fucks sake..why is this shit so stupid?!” Rio asked.

“Here, let me do it..” She said. 

 

Rio’s brain was now full of glitches, lungs stripped of oxygen, every limb in her body went numb or didn’t exist anymore- Rio didn’t know which. In that moment, it was Agatha. She was in her orbit, close enough to wrap arms around or push away. Rio truly preferred the second (She didn’t). 

 

Agatha smirked through her cloudy shield, the glass clearly hadn’t been cleaned in ages. Rio didn’t even want to think if the rest of the helmet was ever washed. If she walked out of here with lice though? That’d be a perfect reason to resent Agatha Harkness for eternity. 

 

“Well? Ready to rage, professor?” Agatha asked. 

 

God, you have no idea..

 

Rio didn’t say anything. Instead, she stormed past her to (Almost) break the door down. She heard Agatha’s little snort behind her, but luckily it was drowned by the blaring music through the speakers. 

 

The tail ending of Dragula by Rob Zombie bounced off the walls. Rio felt her anxiety ease for a moment. She grew up with her father blasting those songs through the car speakers. Her small body flew in the air with each bump and turn, hair flying as she giggled with every word they screamed together. It was a beautiful memory, one that warmed her heart. 

 

She never thought that memory, song, feeling would ever be increased. That was until her head turned over her shoulder, seeing Agatha rocking out with her head banging back and forth. She picked up the baseball bats, lips moving as she chanted the chorus, holding out the one for Rio to take. 

 

And suddenly, Rio hated how Rob Zombie just got ten times better. 

 

The song ended just as Rio took the bat, silence filled the void for three seconds before the brutal guitar of ‘Limp Bizkit - Break Stuff ’ welcomed them to the room with spray paint covering the wall, glass bottles and wooden boxes. A few old style television boxes with half broken laptops on desks.

A scream followed along, glass shards decorated in the air and scattered across the floor. Rio leaned to the side with her arm in the air, shielding herself from the sudden explosion. 

 

She wanted to hate this. Fuck. Rio wanted to feel more annoyed by the second. But as her eyes opened back up to see Agatha smiling like a fool, her laughter contagious over the music as she started to scream the lyrics like it’d be her last words. 

 

She’s..oh my-

 

“C'mon Green Witch!” Agatha yelled over the music, flashing her wide grin over. She gestured with her bat to the laptop on the desk. “Hit that shit like it's all you wanna’ do!”

“So like it's you?!” Rio yelled. 

 

“If that's what you're into” She winked. 

 

Of course…walked myself into that one.

“What’s been pissing you off?” She yelled.

“You!”

“Then think of me, honey!”  

 

It’s been hard not to..

 

She stepped back with her arms folded, leaning against the wall with her smirk never failing to disappear. Rio took in a deep breath, looking back at the laptop while Agatha was on her mind. If you told her a few days ago to stand in a rage room, think of Agatha while smashing devices into pieces- She’d be happy to!

 

Rio would think about the cactus she gifted. How she changed the rules overnight to switch classrooms closer to her own. She’d think of their first meeting when her hopes were lifted only to be crushed by Agatha’s insulting demeanor. Every little thing Rio would think of didn't match to what the thoughts were now.  

 

All she could think about now was the polar opposite. 

 

She thought about Agatha’s smirk no longer pissing her off. It made her stomach flip, cheeks darken a shade of red while she ignored the most embarrassing feature- How her cunt burned and threatened to soak through her boxers (She still wasn’t admitting to that and never would). 

 

The way Agatha now made her laugh, the lazy smile that killed her the night before and just in the parking lot. Those insults she once hated, now she was growing adoration for. 

 

She hated everything. How Agatha was growing on her like moss as if she was a tree unable to stop or resist what was happening to her.

I hate her.

“I hate you!” She yelled back.

“AWE! THAT’S SO KIND OF YOU TO SAY, HONEY!”

 

Agatha dodged to her left as Rio rounded to her side of the desk. The movement took Rio by surprise. Somehow she lost her balance lunging forward, her feet tripping as she stumbled into the wall. Her helmet smacked against it first, shoulder crashed while her knees gave out beneath her. 

 

“Shit, Rio!” Agatha called out. 

 

No humor was in the woman’s tone. Just panic and worry as she ran over. The bat was tossed aside, her knees cracked so hard Rio somewhat heard it over the music. If her mind wasn’t so overwhelmed with the sudden fall, she would’ve made an old person joke about Agatha’s knees (Even if she was the older one herself.

She’s worried about me..

 

I-

‘Miley Cyrus - 7 Things’

“Only fuels my ambition to break more shit with you on my mind, Harkness!”

“Game on, professor!” 

 

Rio grinned. 

 

Game on. 

 

 

About an hour later, they stumble out of the room with laughter dying down between them. Their ears were ringing from the music and every piece of destruction they caused. The muffled silence was a beautiful thing for Rio. She hated when overwhelming noises went on for too long.

“C’mere, helmet head”

Oh my god, stop being a perv-

She was a statue beneath Agatha’s touch. Like the woman before her was medusa. Instead of her eyes, it was her fingers able to turn one into stone.

 

Rio wondered if Agatha could hear her heart pounding. Did she think a thunderstorm was raging through her? Rio wouldn’t be shocked if she was. She felt her blood run cold, not from hatred- just fear. 

 

She was terrified of how close they were. Petrified of Agatha's touch, a simple gaze, how her breath was so close she could feel the chill from it against her lips. Every little thing was overwhelming her and suddenly- 

 

I have to resign before Monday..

 

She’s still worried about the fall I took. That’s it. 

 

There is nothing else about this. Get out of your head, idiot. 

 

“I was wearing a helmet” Rio managed to say, but her voice wasn't as rough as she wanted. “I’m fine” 

 

ANDDDDD, THAT WAS A LIE!

 

Agatha’s eyes shot away. She looked at RIo like a child who had been caught in the candy jar when she shouldn’t have been. The woman visibly swallowed, forcing a little smile.

 

“Yeah..right”

 

Her voice was weak, vacant of any humor or the usual tease lined up behind it and Rio started to think words that shouldn’t exist. Not when it was Agatha related.

 

Wait..was she not thinking about- She must’ve been. She couldn’t be thinking about kiss-

 

“Well,” 

 

Agatha sighed as she pulled away and fuck, Rio missed it instantly. She felt cold without her touch, watching the woman walk across the hall to hang up the helmet. 

 

This was all only because she’s touch deprived, that’s it. 

 

Nothing about Agatha 

 

( Everything about Agatha)

 

“Turn around, let me get the zipper before you get in a fight with that too” 

 

Wait, what? 

 

Rio spun on her heel, hating how Agatha was most definitely a fucking witch. Why did she just cave into her demand? It had to be a spell. A curse Rio would follow every word she said from now on. 

The zipper was pulled down, Agatha’s fingers pushing the texture off Rio’s shoulders. She rushed to take over from there, not letting her go any further before she exploded out of emotion and desire in front of her. 

 

They both moved in silence after the two close interactions…well, maybe three if you count the fall Rio took as well. 

 

“Well,” Agatha sighed. “That felt good, didn’t it?” She asked. 

 

Rio glared. Agatha snickered. 

 

The worker had disappeared from the counter, both silently thankful to leave their gear and head out to the parking lot. Rio this time took the lead to push the door open, holding it for Agatha to walk out from behind. 

 

“Okay, maybe the fall wasn’t great. But, mentally it felt good, no?” She asked, quickly adding, “After being stood up, it was some nice therapy”

 

Rio almost questioned what she meant, completely forgetting the Tinder date she was supposed to go on. Her entire weekend had been taken up by Agatha. The woman lived in Agatha’s mind more than ever before. 

 

This is terrifying..

 

“I guess I’ll…give you that” She shrugged. 

 

The closer they got to Agatha’s car, Rio’s initial plan grew closer. She wanted to leave the second she could. Give Agatha a cold shoulder, Irish goodbye, forget any of this happened by Monday. 

 

However, as they stepped closer to Agatha’s car…Rio felt her heartstrings tugging her mind back. They grew stronger, shifting the organ to the front lines of all her guards that would shield her from Agatha Harkness. 

 

Rio knew she was losing it with the idea swimming in the sea of her thoughts. Tidal waves crashing, whirlpools swirling out of control to the point of a vicious storm of their own. 

Don’t say it. 

 

She shoved her hands in her pockets, lips pulled back. 

 

Do not. 

 

Rio stood up a bit taller, tongue swiping the inside of her cheek slowly, 

 

DON’T FUCKIN-

 

“Hey uh, do you want to go grab a drink or something? I’m..I’m not doing anything after this, so-”

 

“Shit” Agatha muttered. 

 

Told you not to do it..

 

The woman spun around, the phone in her hand seemingly a device that created a panicked look on Agatha’s face. She looked up from the screen, double checking it before taking a frustrated, defeating sigh. 

 

“I gotta’ go” She rushed. 

 

“Oh uh,” Rio brought a hand to rub over the nape of her neck, tugging a few of the tiny roots to create a pinching sensation. “Right..” 

 

Agatha barely said a word. She rushed a few ones that Rio somehow managed to understand. A quick jumble of,

 

“I know. We forget this by Monday. Same old shit, right. Bye” 

 

Her tone was short, leaving Rio stunned as she watched the vehicle fly out of the parking lot. She watched her disappear down the road. Agatha flew away as if she never existed a few steps ahead of her in the first place. 

 

Why would she want to get drinks with you?

This was just so her stupid coupon, thing, whatever didn’t go to waste. 

You hate her. She hates you. That’ll never change. 

 

Rio swallowed the lump in her throat, kicking the tiny pebbles as her feet carried her to the car in defeat. As she fell into her driver’s seat, slamming the door shut and secluding herself from the outside world- That’s when everything hit her all at once. 

 

She felt the stinging in her eyes, stupid tears threatening to coat her cheeks. Her palm lifted to press over her lips, holding her breath as much as she could so the sobs wouldn’t win. 

 

Why did I ask?

Better yet..why did I agree to any of this?

 

“Fuck off, Harkness..” She whispered to herself.  

 

 

Agatha had floored it out of the parking lot the second her Blink camera sent her the front door notification. She figured it was a late Amazon delivery or just a car driving by. But, when she saw the shadow figure sitting on her front porch steps- She knew exactly who it was. 

 

Her car swung into the driveway, coming to an abrupt stop as her head dipped to see the boy sulking into himself. She turned the engine off, shoulders dropped with a low, 

 

“Shit..” 

 

The woman grabbed her purse and phone, jumping out of the car to meet him where he stayed. 

 

“Not good?” She asked.

 

The boy looked up, eyeliner streaks from the tears smudged over his cheeks. A few little gasps were choked as he shook his head. No words were needed between the two. Agatha gestured her finger in the air, stepping around him to unlock the door. 

 

Billy had become Alice’s teaching assistant early last year. Somehow though, he managed to drift over to Agatha and she had taken him under wing. This wasn't the first time he sat by her doorstep with tears in his eyes. 

 

The first time he did, Agatha didn’t know what to do. It was over a fight with his mother and he needed a shoulder to cry on. If anyone knew that would be his move, they’d tell him to stay clear and never do such a thing. 

 

However, Agatha was somewhat happy he did. She didn’t mind being a mentor of sorts. The company to keep around was nice as well. 

 

“Sit,” She ordered, but her voice was soft. “I'll grab you something” 

 

“Agatha..” 

 

“Hm?”

 

She turned around before entering the kitchen. His voice was small, body fragile as his limbs shook and he held onto himself.  Truly, he didn’t need to say anything or ask. Agatha knew him well enough to know what he wanted, more so needed. 

 

“Can..” He held his breath for a moment. “Can I-”

 

“Oh, you didn't just think I was telling you to sit. Did you?” 

 

She asked, pointing over her shoulder down the hallway where the living room sat at the end. 

 

“You should know the meaning of that was you're crashing on the couch tonight. Now, go” Agatha directed, disappearing into the kitchen. 

 

She heard his footsteps patter down the hallway, little sniffles created their own echoing trail. Agatha thought about chasing down the boy who most definitely broke his heart. This had been a battle for months now. A friend of his had flirted, showed signs of wanting more and constantly crushed him over and over. 

 

Little twink. 

 

Billy was head over heels about the boy as well, always making excuses to hang out and find ways to see him. 

 

Agatha was in the middle of filling up a glass of water when she froze, a thought breaking into her mind like an intruder,

 

Just like Rio..

 

She aggressively turned the water off, nearly smacking the cup down on the counter. This wasn’t about her stupid fucking crush on the woman. Tonight was about the emo boy on her couch, a wreck of tears and sorrow. But as she grabbed the package of Oreos, popping one into her mouth- 

 

He’s just like me with this shit..

 

Maybe she had to kick him to the curb, save him from pining over someone for years like she had been doing. 

 

“I’m out of your seltzer shit,” Agatha said as she stepped into the living room. “Water and Oreos will have to do”

 

She hated any drink that was seltzer, but Billy lived off the stupid things. Usually, she had a stash in the pantry for him. But, he had finished the last one the last time he was at her place. Agatha was supposed to grab more at the store, but obviously someone in particular had distracted her from doing so. 

 

“Thank you, Agatha..” He said. 

 

His knees were to his chest, arms locked around with small sniffles. She placed the cup and package down on the coffee table, plopping on the couch beside him. Silence stretched for a few moments between them. Agatha finished chewing down her second Oreo before taking a sigh,

 

“It isn't you..” 

 

She moved her elbow on the back of the couch, head resting against her hand. 

 

“I just don't get it” He said, voice trembling. “I really…we get along and we were flirting and all the signs are there and-” He scoffed. “It’s like..so close..so fucking close and I-”

 

“Sometimes, life is shit. It misdirects and you just gotta’ roll with it” Agatha shrugged. 

 

“But what if I'm tired of rolling with it?” He asked, looking over with exhaustion covering his entire soul. “It’s getting worse now. He..he acts like he hates me in public with our friends. We’re entering an enemy ark to disguise our almost could be one”

 

Ouch. That hits close to home. 

 

Obviously, Agatha couldn’t open up about how well she truly understood every word he said. Each syllable, letter, all of it hit her like darts targeting the bullseye. 

 

“Why are you doing this?” She asked. “Why do you keep putting yourself through the damn thing?” 

 

Are you asking him or yourself?

 

“Because..” He sighed. “I just want it to be him, Agatha. I- I only think about him, I have stupid dreams and it’s like we laugh together and I think this is it, we can be more, and-”

 

He started to choke on his words, gasping for air as he shook his head. 

 

“What is wrong with me? Am I not enough or-”

 

Agatha shushed him while reaching out. She pulled him into her embrace with one arm, feeling his sobs shake every limb that made him his skinny being. 

Can I kill this kid? Then he wouldn’t be putting himself through this.

 

“I wanna’ be like you..” He muffled into the flannel shirt. 

 

Agatha pulled back, forcing him to sit up so they were back to eye level. She narrowed her stare, lips frowned while shaking her head. 

 

“Why-”

 

“You’re strong, you’re smart like..you’d never put yourself through this!” He said. “I’m weak. I can’t stop myself and-”

 

Jesus, kid. You have no idea. You are like me, more than you will ever know. 

 

Agatha shook her head, holding her hand in the air for him to stop. He was silenced instantly. 

 

“You’re..” 

 

She started, not knowing where to go with it. How could she? Agatha was doing the same fucking thing and had no idea how to stop herself. 

 

“Sometimes the stupid Nicholas Sparks crap, shit show infests us” She said. “It’s shitty, sappy, sickening bullshit that organ in our chest wants-”

 

“You mean love, right?” He asked. 

 

“Ew” She cringed. “But yeah, whatever you want to call it”

 

She was happy to see his little smile lift. A tiny puff of air that was a ghost of a laugh came from him. 

 

“We both know logic can only take us so far” Agatha added. “Science hasn’t created a pill to help that-”

 

“Well, technically-”

 

“I’m not talking that crap. This is Nora Roberts territory. Not Stephen King-”

 

“Are you comparing mentally ill people to Stephen King characters?” Billy asked. 

 

Agatha held her hands out to both sides, eyes wide as she shrugged. 

 

“Am I wrong?” She asked. 

 

He rolled his eyes. 

 

“That’s offensive, Agatha”

 

“No, what’s offensive is that little fag leading you on and-”

 

“Jesus, Agatha!” He groaned. “We talked about that word”

 

“Okay? And I’m not in a gay bar surrounded by your little friends to offend” She shrugged. “Also, I’m going to insult that nasty boy of yours. I don’t like him and you know it” 

 

He shook his head, muttering how unbelievable she was, but deep down? Billy adored her for it and Agatha knew it. The boy sat back, hands covering his face as his head tilted behind. A loud groan exhaled before silence sat between them again. 

 

“Do you still have that rage room thing?” He asked. 

 

Rio. 

 

The memory of not even an hour before waved its warm hello. She heard Rio’s laughter in her mind, the smile wide as how those brown orbs sparkled when she touched her up close. The hour had flown by faster than any hour of her lifetime. 

 

Agatha never wanted to leave that room. She never wanted to leave Rio’s side. When they walked out to the parking lot, the impending doom was a portal she stepped through. Rio had been saying something behind her back. Most likely an insult or her chance to make a quick escape. 

 

No. 

 

The words she spoke were definitely about Monday. Rio had been a broken record, saying the order on repeat that put Agatha's heart through the shredder every single time. 

 

Maybe Billy crying on her front porch steps made him her savior from hearing that painful speech once more. Agatha wasn’t sure if she could stomach it after being with her. Billy’s words hit hard, they were painfully true. Worse than Agatha could imagine. 

 

We get along. 

We laugh. 

She clearly is flustered when I flirt. 

 

Why can’t we just fucking do it?

 

I’m not enough for her. 

She’s way too good for me to ever have. 

I couldn’t treat her how she deserves. 

 

Maybe it’s all for the best.

 

“Did you forget about it?” 

 

About Rio? Never.

 

Agatha flipped her head back, eyes wide as she struggled to figure out what he was asking. Her thoughts still bounced like jumping beans, flip flopping at a rapid pace. 

 

“Forget what?” She asked. 

 

He tilted his head to the side, eyes narrowed in on her. 

 

“The rage room- Have you not been listening again? I know you hate Nora Roberts, but-”

 

“Yes! Yes, sorry uh- Had to think about it. You know Nora Roberts, what that wicked woman does to me”

 

Billy scoffed.

 

“Right. She only wrote some of the best books imaginable with pissing specifically you off” He argued. “It’s not that you have the worst shopping addiction or anything”

 

Her jaw dropped, hand over her heart with a sharp gasp,

 

“Do you not benefit from my shopping sprees?! I dare say, that gay little wardrobe of yours has excelled since meeting me” She stood up, brushing the Oreos crumbs off her shirt as she muttered, “Not to mention, saved you from those horrendous khakis” 

 

“Oh, come on!” He laughed. “I looked adorable in them!” 

 

“Your definition of adorable and mine hold entire different meanings” 

 

“Shocker there..” 

 

She smirked his way before finding the local pizza shop’s menu on the coffee table. In the mess of magazines, books and random puzzle pieces it laid- never needing to be used from how the shop knew her by name, but it was the principal of it. A routine and tradition that must be followed. 

 

“Here,” She tossed the paper in his lap. “Find us something good to watch, order whatever- I’ve got cash”

 

“No, Agatha. I’ll pay, I intru-”

 

Agatha held her head up high as she exited the room, singing a loud,

 

“LALALA! I CAN'T HEAR YOUUUU” 

 

She heard his laugh, smiling softly to herself for being able to pull him from the tears. Even if it was only momentarily he was able to breathe, better than not having a second at all.

 

Agatha shut the bathroom door behind her, letting go of a breath she hadn’t even realized had been held in. Her hands rested on the edge of the sink, head hanging low as if she could let the thoughts fall into the drain below. 

 

How Rio’s smile was bright. 

How Rio’s laugh was contagious. 

How Rio’s way of keeping Agatha on her toes, going head to head with her sarcastic wit. 

 

Rio. Rio. Rio. 

 

Three fucking years, a stupid mistake Agatha still dwelled on from their first meeting. Her mother always said people would see the bad in her one way or another. She also reminded Agatha of how evil, cruel, a fuck up she truly was. 

 

That was all proven horribly true the first night she laid eyes on the beautiful woman.

 

“This usually work for you?” Rio gestured between them. “Just…insulting someone off the bat?” 

 

Agatha clicked her tongue, head tilting to the side as she tapped her fingers against the wine glass. 

 

“What? Are you not like other girls?” The woman asked. “Don’t like to be brought back down to earth a little bit?”

 

Rio laughed, rolling her eyes as she shook her head. 

 

“You don’t even know who I am to be making the call if I need to be brought back down to earth to begin with” She argued.

“I know ‘em when I see ‘em” Agatha shrugged. 

 

The memory of their first meeting haunted her with every glare, every argument, every insult tossed like a hot potato back and forth. 

 

God, why did you have to say that? 

 

She had asked herself that for three years, always trying to correct her wrongs, but failing to do so at every turn. How could she play nice twenty four seven when Rio never bothered to try herself? Gifting her a cactus, poking the bear to make her growl louder, talking Lilia into moving to a classroom just down the hall to annoy her more-

 

“Why do you keep putting yourself through the damn thing?”

 

The question she had just asked Billy bit her in the ass. Her own mind questioning herself on why she did this. It’d hurt even worse now knowing how good they could have had it. 

 

If Agatha wasn’t a horrible human being.

If she wasn’t vile and evil. 

If only her language wasn’t insults.

 

She’d be the best fucking thing that ever happened to me..

 

“Agatha!” Billy yelled. “Are we doing garlic knots?!”

 

She cleared her throat, rolling her shoulders back while she turned her head over her shoulder. 

 

“No shit, Sherlock Holmes! And, ooo! Why don’t you consider pizza from the pizza shop as well while you’re at it?!”

 

He never responded, probably too busy rolling his eyes and apologizing to the worker if he heard Agatha on the phone (He did). It gave Agatha time to turn her head to the mirror, seeing the mess of a woman covered in self pity and despair. 

 

Monday was around the corner. She just had to survive her first Monday back and fall into the numb habit of continuing on with hating Rio Vidal. Then maybe things would feel lighter than they were right now. She knew well though, no more hanging out one on one. 

 

The time they had was good. Like a snack so delicious, you mindlessly could eat the whole bag. Agatha couldn’t just close the wrapper and place it on the shelf. She was an addict. One who had to ditch the chips all together…ditch Rio, completely. 

 

Agatha nodded to herself, swallowing the lump in her throat,

 

I won’t even acknowledge her come Monday.
Nope. 

Rio Vidal doesn’t exist as far as I’m aware.

 

Even through her tiny pep talk, a plan that’d feel impossible to go through with- But somehow, she’d manage to do so. There was one question Agatha had asked herself for three years and counting, 

 

Why can’t I hate her like she hates me?

That’s What You Get, Your Wish Is True and No Coffee for You

Chapter Notes
