Hangovers, Weed, and Pancakes of Confessions

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

"I've been in love with her for ages
And I can't seem to get it right
I fell in love with her in stages
My whole life

And that's been the way for me to say
That I felt a certain way in stages, oh
I think the story needs more pages, yes"

Slowly, Agatha’s eyes started to blink open, adjusting to the sunlight shining rays beside her. She was partially in the shade, feeling the glow against the side of her face. To her left, a water bottle sat on the coffee table with a bucket on the floor beside it. The atmosphere was peaceful, quiet- 

 

Unfamiliar?

Very, very, unfamiliar. 


Agatha felt her fear kick into gear. She pushed herself up, movements frantic as she tried to piece together not only where she was- But, how she had ended up there. 

 

However, Agatha didn’t have long before-

 

Oh fuck. 

 

She lunged to her side, pulling the plastic bucket to her with one hand while the other gripped the fleece blanket that covered her. Her stomach flipped upside down, inside out, rejecting the remains of what was in her system from the night before. 

 

Agatha hurled, tossed up spews of vomit, felt her body trembling as she struggled to catch her breath. She was distracted by the chaotic few seconds to register the woman behind her. How she gently pulled her hair back, tying it up in a high bun. The way her hands rubbed her upper back, soothing her through the final few spits until her body finally caught itself.

 

She coughed a few more times, cringing at the aftertaste it left on her tongue- desperate to catch her breath. After a few seconds of silence, the bucket was placed back down on the floor- 

That’s when Agatha jumped at the foreign touch. And even worse? A small raspy chuckle came from behind as her hand disappeared from Agatha’s back. 

 

“Well..good morning to you, drunkie” 

 

Holy fuck. 

No. 

Rio? 

Why-

 

“That should tell you how your night went. Bit too much to drink, don’t you think?”

 

Rio grinned as she stepped around the couch, clicking open the water bottle while she handed it to her. 

 

Agatha was stuck in a trance, lips parted as she still tried to catch her breath from being sick- On top of it now was trying to make sense of Rio standing before her. 

 

“C’mon, take this” Rio wiggled the water bottle in the air. “It’ll hel-”

 

“What do you think you’re doing?” Agatha asked. “Better yet, where the fuck am I? What is-”

 

“Like I said, you had too much to drink last night” Rio shrugged. 

 

Agatha stared wide, lips parted as a little scoffed puffed through them.

 

“And so…you took advantage of that and..is this-”

 

“Yes. This is my place” Rio answered. 

 

Agatha's lips turned into a curl of disgust. No. Not a chance in hell was she staying put. She wasn’t staying in Rio’s house or on her couch. There was no way Agatha would stick around Rio any longer. After everything, the last thing she needed was to be near her. That choice would be considered self harm in her eyes.  

 

She snickered, muttering a low. “I’m out of here”

 

And with a spring board shooting her up in the air, Agatha went to push herself up abruptly to her feet, flying out the door at lightning speed.

 

However, that move was abruptly cut short. 

 

Agatha winced as she dropped back onto the couch. She squeezed her eyes shut, head falling into the palm of her hands. Her skull wasn’t just aching. It was full on screaming a loud, fierce amount of pain. She felt off balance, room dizzy while her stomach threatened to make her sick all over again. 

 

Okay..so maybe running away wasn’t in her deck of cards. But, she sure as shit had it in her to tell Rio off. Even if the hangover was wrecking her entire being, emotional pain and anger ran off their own generator.

 

“You’re insane..” Agatha snickered, running a hand through her hair before shooting a glare up at her. “Taking advantage of an intoxicated woman. Don’t you know I can’t consent and-”

 

“Oh my god” Rio laughed in disbelief.

 

She closed the water bottle, tossing it into Agatha’s lap, making the woman jump in her seat. Rio crossed her arms against her chest. She pulled her lips back, nibbling on them. But when Agatha’s lips parted to speak again, Rio beat her to it. 

 

“For starters, we didn’t fuck . Don’t get your hopes up”

 

Agatha felt her body shiver and it wasn’t from being sick, but because those words sparked something in her mind. She felt the memory flicker in spurts of texting words that included ‘Fuck’ and ‘Rio’ but couldn’t quite place them. The night before was still fuzzy, not quite clear to her. 

 

I didn’t tell her I want that..right?

 

“Second- You were fucking wasted, Agatha. I didn’t bring you here to take advantage of you, idiot. I know you hate me and everything, but I am not that kind of disgusting freak”

 

The woman subtly nodded. She couldn’t argue with Rio there. Even with her anger and resentment, Rio wasn’t an evil being. A reason Agatha fell hard despite Rio’s continuous hatred for her. 

 

Rio was kind, soft. A gentle hearted woman right down to her core. Everyone may give her shit for being stubborn and driven, for living by her work. However, every single person who’d ever landed within a foot of Rio Vidal knew- 

 

She’s an angel. A stupid, fucking, angel. 

 

Of course, Rio took in Agatha drunk off her ass even after their fight. 

 

Of course, Agatha was hungover on her couch with a water bottle in her lap and a bucket of vomit in front of her. 

 

Of course, Rio held her hair back and soothed her through getting sick without a blink of an eye. 

 

Of course, she's the one fucking asshole who’d ever take care of me like this. 

 

Fucking hell. 

 

“Third-” Rio held her finger up. “My friend owns the bar you were hanging out at. She called me to tell me you were drunk off your ass”

 

And, that was a lie.

 

Too hungover to question how Lou knew Rio and Agatha were co workers, enemies, whatever they were- She just let the explanation slide, not bothering to press on the answer more. 

 

Instead, her head tipped back as she pinched the bridge of her nose. 

 

“Gotta’ be kidding me..” Agatha muttered, running a hand through her hair before puffing out a tiny laugh. “You’re insane,” She muttered. 

 

“Insane?” Rio asked. “Some people say thank you instead, just a thought”

 

Agatha rolled her eyes, looking around to find her phone. She muttered a few curse words, about to snap and ask Rio where it was. Though as if Rio read her mind, she cleared her throat to earn the woman’s attention. Held in the air before her was her phone, followed by the amused grin from the woman holding it. 

 

“Gimme’ that” 

 

Agatha muttered, reaching up to snatch it from her. However, she missed as Rio held it back with a little, stupid, annoying, giggle. 

 

“Ri-”

 

“I even charged your phone for you. Don’t I deserve a thank you somewhere, Ms Harkness?”

 

Ms Harkness? That’s new..

 

“Waitingggg” Rio sang. 

 

Oh this woman is-

 

“You’re really fucking irritating” Agatha said through gritted teeth. 

 

Rio grinned with a hand over her heart. “Awe! Now you know how I’ve felt for the last three years!” 

 

Oh. I’m fucking sure. 

 

“Sooo,” Rio waved her phone back and forth as if Agatha was a dog and Rio was holding a bone. “What do we say for taking care of you, charging your phone and-”

 

“You’re an asshole”

 

“Mm, close!” Rio hummed. “Come on, you can do it. Be a good girl for me ” 

 

Be a…be a wha-

 

Rio swiped her tongue on the inside of her cheek, slowly licking from bottom to top. She never took her eyes away from Agatha’s, appearing unphased for the two words she dared to say. Agatha on the other hand felt her entire body light on fire. A match was set and placed on a river of gasoline, scorching through her in a matter of seconds. 

 

Was Rio doing this on purpose? Did the fuzzy memory of those texts Agatha sent the night before actually exist? What did Rio know and how the fuck would she survive being trapped until she felt strong enough to leave?

 

Agatha took in a deep breath, muttering a low. “Thank. You.” 

 

The woman above beamed brighter than the sun. She tossed the phone on Agatha’s lap, smiling wide as she chirped a way too loud for a hangover headache to hear-

 

“You’re welcome!” 

 

Agatha cringed, feeling the pulse in her head pound with an ache a bit harder. She thought peacefulness would finally come. THe phone was in her hands, Uber app pulled up to save her from this hell hole. But then, temptation creeped upon her. An offering that sounded far too good to pass up.

 

“Want a cup of coffee?” Rio asked.

 

Agatha snickered. “You planning on poisoning me with it?” 

 

The offer sounded beautiful and Agatha felt the blissful taste of coffee on her tongue, but..she couldn’t show Rio that excitement. She was already giving her hell left and right as it was. 

 

Rio rolled her eyes. “Yes, you caught me” 

 

She put her hands up in surrender, feigning theatrics that nearly mirrored the ones Agatha always gave her. 

 

“Making sure you're safe and taken care of is all a ploy, a con! Just to poison your sorry ass” 

 

Agatha scoffed, narrowing her eyes on the woman with an annoyed, 

 

“You're enjoying this too much” 

 

Rio grinned. “Agatha, as long as your hungover ass is on my couch-” 

 

She leaned down, a smirk wider than the devil's while her voice deepened into something low. A raspy tone that sent shivers down Agatha’s spine.  

 

“I'm just getting started..” Rio winked. 

 

And as if Rio was never in her orbit, far too close to her as she sped through every warning and stop sign- The woman pulled back before Agatha was able to take a breath. She hummed a soft tune while walking away, leaving Agatha to close her eyes and take a heavy sigh. 

 

She’s killing me. 

This hangover won’t be the death of me- Rio will fucking be. 

 

She opened her phone, checking messages first. Only Billy had sent her a few about how his Tinder date was going. The latest update being he left early because the boy made him uncomfortable. 

 

“Shit” Agatha muttered to herself, thumbs tapping across the keyboard. 

 

Usually when dates went bad, Agatha was his savior. She’d show up unannounced without Billy’s request to drag him away. Sometimes she’d fake an emergency, other times she just took him away while the date was in the bathroom. Anytime Billy didn’t feel safe, Agatha would shoot out of bed- Even in her pajamas to get to him. 

 

And this time, she was too busy drinking away every piece of Rio. Well, tried anyway. 

 

She sent a small text about how they’d talk soon and to delete the app for now. It wasn’t worth putting himself through date after date when he still had that other boy on his mind. Agatha knew far too well a string of hook ups, useless dates to try and ignore that certain someone made things worse. At least, for her it did. 

 

Just as she hit send, a plastic package smacked against her phone. She jumped, head snapped to the source with a pain that shot like a million bullets. Rio was opening a bottle of pain meds, not paying attention to her as she still hummed that stupid, annoying, tune. Agatha looked down, flipping the package over,

 

“That doesn’t look like coffee” She said. 

 

It was a purple toothbrush, her favorite color. Did Rio do that on purpose? No. Not a chance. Why would she?

 

“Oh, so you like the taste of vomit on your tongue?” Rio asked, snapping her fingers right after. “Right! How could I forget the delicious combination of vomit and coffee!” 

 

Agatha scrunched her nose, hating being reminded of what happened the second she woke up. Rio handed her the two pills of aspirin. Agatha took it without an argument or even a thank you. 

 

“Bathroom is the first door on the left, can’t miss it” Rio directed. 

 

She leaned down to grab the bucket and this time, Agatha wasn’t arguing in a malicious or annoyed way. 

 

“No, no- I’ve got that, Rio. Seriously, I-”

 

“Shut it” Rio ordered. 

 

Embarrassment wasn’t only covering Agatha’s tone, but she physically felt it taking over the hangover’s pain. 

 

From passing out drunk on her enemy’s couch, waking up sick and hungover in the same spot- And now Rio, the woman who was her enemy and someone she couldn’t stop falling in love with cleaning up her vomit..

 

“Rio-”

 

“Toothpaste is on the sink” Rio said.

 

She paused with the bucket held in her hand by her side as Agatha’s cheeks tainted a deep shade of red. The way she looked down, fiddling with the toothbrush packet in her hands. 

 

“Agatha..” Rio softened, offering a tiny smile. “I clean up dog shit and vomit. I really won’t blink an eye over this. Besides, don’t need you getting sick from cleaning up your own vomit”

 

Agatha puffed out a small laugh. One that was weak and filled with defeat. 

 

“C’mon now,” Rio kicked her foot out, softly tapping it against Agatha’s leg. “Go brush your teeth, splash some water on your face. It’ll help”

 

Rio continued to hum as she walked away, leaving Agatha to debate getting up or to stay put. Ultimately, the aftertaste of sour, bitter, with leftover whiskey (Or, she was probably just imagining that) won. She pushed to her feet to patter down the hall. 

 

The bathroom was easy to find as Rio told her it would be. She shut the door behind her, giving herself the privacy to use the toilet and wash up. Her bladder was emptied, teeth brushed, face soaked in cold water and dried off- 

 

Shit. 

 

Agatha caught herself staring at her own reflection. Pale skin, darkened eyes with heavy bags underneath. Her hair was a wreck, clothes wrinkled and worn out. Agatha was worn out. 

 

Is this rock bottom? She wondered.

Agatha wasn’t an alcoholic, but she was self destructive. After the first week of silence and barely ever seeing Rio, the fight they had in the parking lot- She felt herself slowly losing every glue, every thread, all the bricks that kept her wall together being destroyed. 

 

How can I be heartbroken over someone that was never mine to begin with?

 

She asked herself that question every now and then, but now it was more than ever. Like clockwork, intuition on the other woman’s part as if she knew Agatha was starting to think of her- Two knocks on the bathroom door snapped her back into reality. 

 

Agatha cleared her throat, rolling her shoulders back as she hung the hand towel back up.

 

“What do you want?” She asked. 

 

“I have a set of more comfortable clothes if you want” Rio offered. 

 

Why?

 

The one word started to scream in her mind. Had Rio lost it or was this some wicked vivid dream? Their fight on Friday was brutal, Rio made it clear she wished things would have been different. She said the words that made Agatha freeze and cry driving home that night. How she thought them never talking, meeting, should have been the way everything was.

 

So why the hell was she being nice all of the sudden?

 

Agatha reached out, ripping the door open with a rough,

 

“Why are you doing this?” 

 

Rio’s mouth had moved to say something, but shut as Agatha took the floor instead. 

 

She stood with a neatly folded set of clothes in her arms. What looked like a black hoodie, green sweatpants underneath. Agatha knew deep down they didn’t look comfortable solely because she was exhausted, hungover, and her clothes from the night before felt disgusting. Reality was, they were Rio’s. 

 

The thought of not only being in Rio’s home, on her couch, staying the night even if the memory of it was fuzzy- But to add on wearing her clothes? 

 

I’m signing my death certificate if I agree to this. 

 

Rio shrugged. “I hate hangovers” 

 

Agatha stared, eyes squinted for a few seconds before a tiny scoff,

 

“Okay? We all do, so why are you-”

 

Rio muttered something incoherent under her breath. A few words not spoken in English. Agatha only heard her speak Spanish a few times over the three years of knowing her, but fuck. She’d be lying if she said it didn’t make Rio hotter than she already was. 

 

“What was that?” Agatha asked, trying her best to stay angry and cold. 

 

Rio sighed. “Just…take these, alright?”

 

“Rio..” Agatha laughed. “Answer the fucking question”

 

“Why are you questioning someone helping you? Huh?”

 

“Because said person just wished we never spoke or met in the first place” 

 

Rio shook her head. “First part, yes. But I never said that about us ever meeting-”

 

“Oh!” Agatha nodded. “Right. K’, that makes it so much better” She rolled her eyes. 

 

The woman’s head looked away, fiddling with the fabric of her hoodie. She started to teeter side to side, rocking on her feet while sticking her tongue in cheek. Agatha felt her own aggressive demeanor weaken. She’d blame the hangover before ever admitting taking pity on Rio. 

 

She sighed, running a hand through her hair. “I’m just confused”

 

Rio huffed with a nod. “Ditto”

 

“What is that supposed to mean?”

 

She looked up, staring for a few lingering moments. Agatha knew they were close. The woman felt it in her bones they were stepping towards an answer, a line that she never thought would be crossed.

 

But then, like a buzzer that declined what Agatha ever wanted- The coffee maker beeped in the kitchen. Both of them jumped subtly in their spot, Rio’s head whipped over before back at Agatha. She nervously chuckled, shoving the clothes against Agatha’s chest. 

 

“So uh, how do you take your coffee? You know what! You always choose my order against my will so…payback for that. K’, cool. Uh, just- I’ll be- Head to the living room after if you want”

 

And as if Rio was never there, she rushed down the hall and disappeared back in the kitchen. She left Agatha holding onto the clothes, staring wide as she muttered under her breath, 

 

“I like my coffee with answers..” 

 

She stepped back, shutting the door while placing the clothes on the edge of the sink. Her phone lit up, distracting her for just a few seconds. It was Billy sending a meme of a sad gif. Some kid walking before falling face first. She scoffed, quickly shooting back how the boy he adored was missing out. 

 

Though before putting her phone back down, she opened Instagram to check the reels Alice had sent her. Yet…that never happened. Her heart sank, finding Rio’s last message being a simple,

 

“Agatha?” 

 

Agatha tapped the screen, feeling sick with anxiety as she saw her own messages one after the other. She scrolled up through them, quickly noticing how Rio lied to her moments prior. 

 

Lou never called Rio. 

She didn’t know they knew each other. 

 

Rio not only was searching for her, but Agatha had texted her drunk off her ass. Agatha wasn’t sure which one was worse. 

 

“Wait..” She whispered. 

 

“Don’t tele” 

 

She nibbled on her bottom lip. 

 

Don’t tell who..what? 

 

The one above that caught her eye was even more confusing. 

 

“I’m sorry I should nt say”

 

Agatha scoffed. 

 

“Shouldn’t say what?” She asked herself. 

 

The first half of the messages were in order and made sense. However the second half?

 

Something is off…

 

She felt the fuzzy memories of drunken messages hit her. The ones Agatha had been questioning their existence or not. And like a punch, an explosion-

 

“Oh fuck” She muttered. 

 

They all registered in her mind, beeping with a scanner each time they appeared. 

“I think if we matched on Tinder” 

“Wasting time on you” 

“Would you be jealous if I fucked her?”

“I’d rather fuck you” 

“Did you fuck her?” 

“Why not me?”

Agatha dropped her phone on top of the clothes. She pressed the back of her hand over her mouth, the other gripping her hip with such force she threatened to crush the bone. 

Those messages were real. Their placements lined up the drunken mess of texts perfectly. Puzzle pieces scattered that slotted into their spots in order. Agatha had sent the most damning texts of her lifetime. Ones she’d regret for eternity. 

But, she deleted them. How on earth did she delete those? 

For starters, Agatha knew herself well enough to know when she was too far gone. Drunk texting the enemy you hopelessly had fallen for was a clear enough sign. Not remembering exactly how she ended up on Rio’s couch? Another. Both of them told her over and over the same thing.

I couldn’t have deleted these..

There’s no way I was drunk texting her and remembering to delete them.

Agatha shook her head, hand running through the tangled mess of hair. 

“How..” She muttered. “I-”

“I even charged your phone for you. Don’t I deserve a thank you somewhere, Ms Harkness?”

 

Rio’s voice echoed in her mind. Agatha thought those words over, thinking about how she kept her phone unlocked right after. Billy always said that was a poor decision, but she never cared. No one was ever around to have a reason to take her phone. If some criminal who stole her shit wanted to, he wouldn’t find anything interesting either in her eyes. 

 

She deleted them..she-

 

Agatha started to nervously laugh under her breath. She paced back and forth in the tiny bathroom, tugging at the roots of her hair- threatening to yank them out of her skull. 

 

“Okay, two reasons..one could be true and the other night” She whispered to herself.

 

It wasn’t uncommon for Agatha to ramble on to herself. Sometimes her thoughts were too loud to keep locked in her mind. 

 

“She either hates you texted those or thought I was lying. Drunk off my ass, yeah. That…that could be, but, but, but oh- Shit, shit” She cursed to herself, leaning back as she smacked her thigh a few times. “There’s no way she’d take care of me- Not-”

 

Agatha shook her head, voice cutting off as two words rang in her mind,

 

“Good girl”

 

“That was flirting” She muttered to herself, but then shook her head. “No” She scoffed with a pathetic laugh. “She wouldn’t…but she never has talked to me like that before. She never-”

 

This was a mess. One giant fucking mess Agatha had no idea where to find the cleaning supplies for. At the rate they were going, bleach and a mop didn’t exist. Agatha knew she was being left to her own devices to clean this up. 

 

She looked back at the clothes, feeling her flannel and jeans far too tight. Agatha was already suffocating in fear and adrenaline, confusion piling on top of everything else. For a split moment, she debated getting an Uber and the hell out of here but…

 

Good girl. 

 

That was a clear indication of flirting. Agatha may live in a state of denial at times, but she knew the meaning of what was said. And the fact Rio had never spoken to her like that before? If those texts were real (Which Agatha was 110% they were) and all of the sudden, Rio was using those words? 

 

She thought as well how minutes ago, Rio almost said something- Gave her just a hint of an answer, but that stupid fucking coffee maker took it away. 

 

Fuck it. 

 

Agatha wasn’t going to run from this. What more damage could staying possibly do? She was already drowning, sinking past the ocean floor over every little thing about Rio. Rio on the other hand would easily slip back into hating her and would expect another weekend to be forgotten. 

 

She stripped her clothes, folding them into a pile before pulling on the set Rio gave her. 

 

The pants were soft, comfortable and fit perfectly. No issue there. 

 

The hoodie? There was one major issue and it most certainly was not how it fit. 

 

“Fuck..” Agatha muttered. 

 

The smell of Rio swallowed her, stole her, took her in like she was its next victim. 

 

She always loved the cologne that could only be described as an apple, woodsy smell. But her clothes? Agatha never knew how comforting, addictive, better than that stupid cologne it could smell. 

 

The soft laundry detergent laced with an earthy, sweet, grounding fragrance that instantly calmed the storm raging inside of her. She lowered her head, gripped the edge of the sink to catch her breath. 

 

God, I hate her..

 

She didn’t, she really fucking didn’t. What Agatha hated was even with the pain Rio inflicted on her, how the last three years had been an endless hell- The stupid smell of her clothes could ease every inch of the adrenaline in her. How being in her home was comforting even through the urge to run at any given moment. 

 

And she hated her for deleting those texts and not knowing why. 

 

Agatha looked back up in the mirror, taking in a deep breath and mentally counting down to get back out there. The smell of coffee lingering through the door helped with the motivation to do so.

 

Five. 

 

Just gotta’ figure out what the motive was for that. 

 

Four. 

 

Also why the hell she’s taking care of me.

 

Three. 

 

Worst comes to worse, I just quit my job and leave the country. 

 

Two. 

 

She already hates me, fuck it. I can’t make it worse than it already is. 

One. 


Showtime. 

 

Agatha pushed herself back up, grabbing her clothes off the sink before leaving the room. She nearly stormed down the hall, stomping with determination in every step. 

 

Just as she entered the living room, Rio was sitting on the other end of the couch with the coffee mug in her hand. She looked up, offering it to her as she spoke,

 

“Alright, coffee for-”

 

“Liar!” Agatha exclaimed. 

 

Great start. Maybe should’ve planned this out more. 

 

Rio paused, eyebrows furrowed over the word.  

 

“Uh,” She looked in the mug, shaking her head. “Nope. Definitely coffee” 

 

“If your friend called you..” Agatha held her phone up with a low smile. “Why did you interrogate me on my whereabouts?” 

 

Rio’s cheeks burned, shading a deep flush that Agatha swore she felt the heat radiating off of from across the room. She looked down, leaning forward to rest the coffee on the table. It was clear Agatha had caught her in a lie and Rio knew it. 

 

Now..this is fun. Agatha thought to herself.

 

“You know, I was going to question how Lou knew we were…what? Co workers? Enemies? Besties-”

 

Rio sighed, rolling her eyes as she sat back. She folded her arms against her chest, clearly unamused by Agatha’s words. 

 

“But when I opened these messages- It all clicked!” Agatha grinned.

 

Rio scoffed, shaking her head.

 

“You know, you are far too giddy for the one who drunk texted me” 

 

“Yes, but!” Agatha held her finger up, taking slow steps over to the couch. “I did not lie about how you found me” 

 

And deleted those messages, but…we’ll get to that. 

 

Rio watched her every move carefully, evidently more nervous by the second. With every word, every step- 

 

“Do you want the stupid coffee or not?” Rio asked. 

 

“Oo, feisty” Agatha smirked. “What? Don’t like being caught in a lie?”

 

“Maybe I was just trying to make you feel better. Save your ego from feeling the damage of drunk texting me” 

 

“Oh honey..” Agatha rasped with a small grin. 

 

She leaned down to pick the coffee mug up, her body just a few inches away from Rio’s. Agatha mirrored the scene Rio had given her prior. Where she had leaned over her, saying how she was just getting started before rushing away as if she was never there. 

 

Could that be classified as flirting too? Agatha wondered. 

 

Her head turned, lips curled into a dangerous smile that made Rio sink into the couch a bit more. 

 

“You came running to my rescue. Think your ego is taking a stronger hit over mine”

 

Agatha swiftly pulled away, dropping on the other end of the couch with a proud grin. One full of herself that earned a glare from the other woman. 

 

She took a sip of the coffee, about to boast about how Rio making her the cup was another thing to ruin her ego. However, the taste silenced her and not in a bad way. 

 

The coffee wasn’t just good, no…it was, perfect. Better than Agatha made it for herself or any barista she went to. She took another sip, and then another, about to find the strength to tease Rio again. The little snicker on her left beat her to it.

 

“So? Did I guess your order right?”

 

Agatha swallowed the liquid with a shake of her head. 

 

“No-”

 

“Two spoonfuls of sugar, bit of milk and a little bit of caramel,” Rio listed the recipe off. 

 

She’s right. God dammit.

 

Agatha scoffed. “Your ego should feel damaged knowing that”

 

“Interesting way of saying I’m right” Rio smirked. 

 

Agatha rolled her eyes, letting the silence linger for a bit. Rio had pulled her phone out as Agatha studied the plants around the room. All bright green, names she didn’t know- Only described as plants or creatures in Rio’s world. 

 

She knew she should press more on why Rio lied, but those deleted drunk text messages started to shove their way to the forefront of everything else. 

 

Part two, get a move on. 

 

Agatha encouraged herself to continue on while she could. Courage was always something Agatha could easily lose. She knew she had to get a move on, take advantage of it before the feeling was stripped away. 

 

“I feel like I texted you about other things…did I?” She blurted.

 

Out of the corner of her eye, Rio was frozen. Her thumbs that had been texting on her screen had come to a stop. She didn’t look up, not a word or movement. The woman was at a complete stand still, a statue with a title, 

 

I deleted them. 

 

Agatha slowly nodded, taking another sip from her coffee. Two options were in front of her. 

 

Option A - Let Rio lie her way out of this. 


Or, 

 

Option B - Call her out on it. 

 

“Nope” Rio lied, popping the p as she pushed back into being nonchalant. No more fear or embarrassment like before. “Just drunken messages about how drunk you were, all that jazz”

 

Jazz? Agatha laughed in her mind. Jesus, you’re a terrible liar. 

 

“Hm” Agatha hummed. “Well-”

 

Before she was able to continue on, Agatha felt a wave of nausea crash like ocean waves over her. She winced, leaning forward to rest the coffee mug on the table and pull her knees up to her chest. Her eyes shut, hands covering her face as she tried to ride it out. 

 

“Stomach again?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha couldn't be bothered with sarcasm at that moment. Instead she muttered a low, 

 

“Nauseous” Agatha muttered. 

 

Rio locked her phone, placing it down on the table not far from Agatha’s phone. Her body shifted a bit, elbows resting on her knees as her fingers picked the skin off her thumbnail. She bounced her knee, clearly stuck in a small debate, a battle in her mind. If Agatha didn’t feel so sick, wasn’t focused on coming down from the feeling- She’d make fun of her.

 

“Wanna’ smoke?” 

 

The question caught Agatha off guard stronger than waking up in Rio’s house did. She looked up, finding a tiny smirk shining bright her way. 

 

“It helps..” Rio shrugged. “I have some light shit. Not strong enough to get you super stoned, but…it’ll ease your stomach” Rio explained, but then snapped her fingers with a fast “Oh! But side effects may include wanting to order food” 

 

Agatha tried to not smile. She really, really, fucking tried. But, the little smirk, snap of her fingers with the tiny side effect she included. God. She hated how stupid Rio’s cuteness was.

 

A little grin escaped from the restraints. She whispered a low, 

 

“I never argue free weed” 

 

“Who said it’s free?” Rio questioned. 

 

Agatha’s smile faded, embarrassment control all over again. She sounded selfish, ashamed of thinking Rio would just smoke her up for free after being such a bitch since she opened her eyes. 

 

Rio stood up, a warm grin took over the smirk as she pointed,

 

“Your payment will be ordering us food”

 

Oh. 

 

Agatha felt her body relax into the couch, she took a small breath, letting go of the shame that was threatening to control her. Slowly, she nodded. A little shrug as she rasped a low,

 

“That can be arranged”

 

Rio nodded. “We have a deal then?”

 

“Stop stalling and medicate me” Agatha ordered. 

 

“Bossy” Rio held her hands up as she walked away. 

 

She picked her phone back up, opening Facebook to scroll through the mess of those posts. Old memes, people in their town group complaining about different neighbors (Agatha did enjoy those the most), but it only kept her mind busy for a few moments. 

 

The giant elephant in her brain grew larger and stronger, spelling out the words, 

 

We won’t be sober. 

 

Agatha blew out a quick stream of air from her nostrils. She put her phone down, pinching the bridge of her nose.

 

I really should just leave. 

 

We didn’t even get to finish- Did we even talk? Why aren’t we finishing anything?

 

Rio wouldn’t answer her question from before. Agatha had caught her in two lies, but nothing was completed or sorted from that. And now they were just going to smoke as if nothing ever happened? 

 

I gotta’ get out of-

 

“Oof!” Agatha yelled out. 

 

She looked down to the heavy weight that had assaulted her. A wide grin, bad breath, tail wagging back and forth in the air. Agatha knew Rio had a dog, everyone did. But, she had yet to truly meet him until he was right on the couch in her face. 

 

Agatha felt her worries wash away. Every thought about fleeing disappeared. She reached up, holding both sides of his face as she scratched his ears.

 

“Well, hi there” She grinned. “Aren’t you a cutie?” 

 

Completely forgetting where she was, too focused on the dog trying to lick her nose while smiling like a lunatic- Agatha didn’t hear Rio rush back into the living room.

 

“Shit, I'm sorry. I'm so used to leaving the back door open for him to run in and out. He's-”

 

“A demon!” Agatha grinned, voice muffled against his fur. “A cute one though, I'd argue” 

 

Agatha pressed her forehead against Nicky’s head. She started to speak in a baby voice about how good of a boy he was, how cute and soft his fur was. 

 

And Rio never knew she could feel so doomed seeing someone with her dog before.

 

Rio's heart stopped at the sight. Agatha sitting up on the couch with her legs tucked under her. Nicky in her lap, both in their own world. How the normally shy puppy’s tail was wagging so fast she wondered if he’d start to float in the air. 

 

It almost felt normal, as if the scene was something that fit their narrative. A story the two were meant to write, a movie they should be in, a life they were meant to live instead of the confusing one they kept on going with. 

 

“Almost makes up for dealing with your wicked, horrible, insufferable mother” Agatha whispered. 

 

Rio scoffed, but was thankful Agatha pulled her away from the spot she was stuck in. She sat down on the other end of the couch, opening the small tin case filled with fresh tiny joints. 

 

“Run along” Rio reached over to tap Nicky’s leg. “You can come suffocate her after we smoke”

 

Agatha hummed, kissing the top of his head before sending him off. 

 

“Such a responsible dog mom, you are” She said.


Rio snickered. 

 

“What?” She asked, placing the joint between her lips. “Think my cruelness extends to my son?”

 

Agatha turned in her spot, elbow rested on the back of the couch with her hand tangled in her hair. 

 

“Oh god, you’re that kind of person?”

 

She watched as Rio flicked the lighter, bringing the flame to the tip. A stream of smoke clouded around it. The woman laughed, coughing a bit as she choked on the smoke. 

 

“You just called me a dog mom” Rio said, passing her the joint. “Hypocrite”

 

Agatha rolled her eyes, eagerly taking the joint and was quick to take not just a hit- But, a deep one. A long drag that she didn’t know she needed so bad. 

 

Rio moved to grab her phone as Agatha smoked. She pulled up a playlist on Spotify, connecting it to the speakers by the TV. The first song, Dreams by The Cranberries, left Rio thankful it wasn’t anything that could relate to them (Well…so she thought). 

 

“How do you know Lou?” Agatha asked, passing the joint back over to Rio. 

 

“College,” Rio shrugged. “You a regular for her?” She smirked a bit. 

 

Agatha sneered, scrunched nose with a little shake of her head as she mocked, 

 

“You a regular for her? Fuck off, Vidal” She muttered. 

 

Rio laughed, taking a slow drag before passing it back to Agatha. 

 

“An old fling..” Agatha shrugged. 

 

That was a lie. 

 

Agatha partially blamed the weed even if she didn’t feel its effects quite yet. She wasn’t going to continue on with edging every conversation they had so far. If Agatha was going to sit here smoking with Rio, listening to music and spending time with her all over again- 

 

She was going to get all the answers before having to act as if this never happened. 

 

“Jealous?” Agatha dared to ask. 

 

Rio laughed, but it didn’t sound like one with humor. It sounded like a defense. A coping mechanism that was protecting the truth behind it. 

 

“Totally” She took a deep inhale of the smoke before passing it back. 

 

Agatha took the joint from her fingers, taking a hit as she replied with a small,

 

“Hm”

 

“What’s hm?” Rio asked. 

 

Agatha held the smoke in her lungs as she shook her head. “Not buying it” 

Rio laughed. “Good. I’m not selling anything for you to buy”

 

“What a shame” Agatha sighed. 

 

The joint was passed a few more times. Only the music filled the silence, neither dared to say another word. 

 

However, the weed started to kick in. Little giggling slipped their lips as Rio stammered,

Stupid fucking weed. 

 

Why did she even suggest smoking? Rio was smart enough to know weed stripped her of a filter, sent her on nonstop rambles with no barriers to stop her. 

 

“I fucking hate you because I can’t stop thinking about..”

 

She holds her breath, desperate to stop herself. Yet..she was too far gone.

On Agatha’s end, she had thought about running and silently cursed how no conversation was finished. Only one felt somewhat secure by the end of it. And now here they were, thrown into confessions and words she never thought they’d hear. 

 

And on Rio’s side of things? All she could explain it would be just a little,

 

“Lol. What did I do?” She’d ask herself after Agatha inevitably left. 

 

Rio didn't know what else to say. She stared up at Agatha who’s shoes were on, belongings in her hands, close to ordering an Uber or just walking home- Both sounded horrible.

“Rio..” Agatha shook her head. “I’m tired. Okay? What are you saying? Just tell me, straight up- Do you want me to stay or go?”

 

Rio stared up, feeling her entire body pulse with desire. The answer was clear, but she was unsure if she’d be able to finally say the truth or not. 

 

She opened her mouth to take in a breath before whispering the first word till the others followed suit,

 

“Agatha..”

Wrong thing, dumbass..

Rio’s phone lit up, Agatha’s name bright on the screen. She had added her number to Rio’s contact list before taking off that night. A subtle way of reassuring their night wasn’t a one time deal. 

 

She smirked slightly to herself, clicking the answer button as she brought it up to her ear.

 

“Booty call already?” Rio asked.

 

A warm laugh graced her ear from the other line. Suddenly, Rio didn’t feel so cold in her own home anymore. 

 

“Don’t get your hopes up, toots” She said. “I’m just looking to ask if I left something at your place”

 

Rio looked around the living room, seeing if any of Agatha’s belongings were anywhere as she asked,

 

“Uhh, what are you looking for? I’m not seeing any-”

 

“My hair tie”

 

Rio stopped her words, movements paused as she registered the object Agatha was looking for. 

 

She sat up, a hand rubbing the back of her neck as she asked, “Your… hair tie? ”

 

“Yes, yes” Agatha sighed as if it was the most devastating loss in the world. “It’s my lucky one. The one” 

 

Rio slowly smirked. She’s bullshitting. Has to be.

 

“Is it there?” Agatha questioned. 

 

Rio looked on her wrist at her hair tie with a little smirk. Obviously, the accessory didn't belong to Agatha’s. But, curiosity got the best of her. If Agatha was bullshitting, lying through her teeth- She wouldn’t question who the hair tie actually belonged to. 

 

“Ah-ha!” Rio faked the sound of finding it. “Well, would you look at that. It is here. Want me to bring it to you tomorr-”

 

“I’ll just come back over to grab it. Lucky one and all” Agatha rushed. 

 

“Are you su-”

 

“I’m grabbing my keys and such right now. See you in a bit?”

 

Rio smiled softly, hating and loving the giddy feeling coursing through her at the idea of seeing Agatha sooner than tomorrow. 

 

But, she still sighed- trying to hide her excitement. “If you insist” 

 

“I insist, insist” Agatha said. “K’, coming over”

 

“I’ll be here” 

 

“Keep my hair tie safe for me”

 

“Oh, I will,” Rio smiled. 

 

Rio opened the door, the sound of the pouring rain louder as it crashed on her porch roof and world around her. Though it was all muted, a muffled sound as the woman before her smiled wide. She was in black sweatpants with a raincoat over her body, not showing a sign of tiredness or being bothered by collecting her cherished lost item. 

 

She held the black hair tie up with a smirk. “Looking for this?”

 

Agatha dramatically sighed, knees caved as she pumped her fists in the air.

 

“Oh! There you are” She beamed, taking it from her hand to slip over her wrist. “Been looking everywhere for you”

 

Rio snickered, finding far too much amusement at the sight of her theatrical show. She didn't need Agatha to confess to how the hair tie was all a lie. A scheme Rio wondered how long it took for her to plot before putting it into action. 

 

“Thank you..” Agatha said, looking behind at the pouring rain with yet another dramatic sigh. “I guess I should get going before the rain is even worse. I always hate driving in it and-”

 

“Agatha..” Rio said. 

 

Agatha whipped around, about to say something when Rio stepped aside with a low,

 

“Just get in here”

 

“Ugh, thank you” Agatha groaned, taking her jacket off as she walked inside. “I wasn’t sure how much longer I could keep that fuckin’ charade going” 

 

The door swung shut, Rio didn’t hesitate to grab Agatha’s hips the second the coat was hung up. She smirked, face inches away from the woman who was rubbing her hands up over Rio’s shoulders. 

 

“Lucky hair tie, huh?” 

 

“Oh very, look where I am..” Agatha smirked. 

 

Just as Agatha was about to kiss her, Rio pulled back with a little shake of her head. 

 

“Funny thing though..” Rio said. “That’s my hair tie” 

 

Agatha’s grin faded, red flooded her cheeks as she bit down on her lips. 

 

“So uh,” She stammered, putting on a tiny grin as she sang. “Busted, disgusted, never to be trusted?”

 

Rio grinned. “Big time” 

 

“Complaints?” Agatha questioned.

 

“Not a single one,” Rio replied. 

 

Agatha pulled her in for a soft, delicate, kiss. Both sighed with relief as if they had gone without one another for years again. Before things were able to progress, become too heavy, Agatha pushed her back to whisper,

 

“I’d still argue it’s a lucky hair tie”

 

Rio paused before a little laugh as she shook her head. 

 

“Just fuck me, Harkness” She ordered.

 

Agatha sighed, slightly pushing her back for them to stumble along the same trail all over again. 

 

“As you wish..”

 

 

The rest of the week had flown by in the blink of an eye. Rio wasn’t completely surprised to find out the night of the hair tie trick, Agatha had an overnight bag packed in her car- determined to not leave until she had to. Unsurprisingly as well, she only left for work a few minutes after Rio. 

 

Both agreed to keep things under the table. They arrived at their usual times, but their banter was noticeably absent. Well, to everyone else. To the two of them, they were doing an excellent job at hiding the very obvious. 

 

Agatha had started to steal Rio’s clothes by Wednesday night when she was out of her own. She took from the back of the closet in hopes people wouldn’t recognize the articles of clothing worn by Professor Vidal first. That didn’t help the two keep their appearance normal. Not when it caused Rio’s staring to be more than usual, stuck in a trance for how good Agatha looked in her clothes. 

 

It wasn’t just the way she owned them, looking marvelous beyond words could ever say. But, Rio felt a sense of pride. Almost as if Agatha was her own to keep. Her clothes were a little mark and claim she had. 

 

And part of Rio slowly lost care if people noticed the clothes belonged to her. 

 

Their nights slowly shifted into a routine. They’d both get home around the same time, stumble into the shower together- Maybe end up in bed with dinner being forgotten. They’d play in the backyard with Nicky, both laughing as they ended up tackling each other instead.


Or, it’d be like where they currently sat. Both on the couch with yet another binge of Law and Order on the TV. Bowls of ice cream sat in their lap, bickering over who was right about how the episode would end. 

 

“Can I have more sprinkles?” Agatha asked.

 

Rio looked over, a little smile as she shook her head. 

 

“I told you to pour more than just that, but no-no! Why listen to little old me-” She said. 

 

Agatha picked up her leg off of the woman’s lap, kicked her foot against Rio’s chest, earning a small, 

 

“Oof!”

 

“Ridiculous” Rio muttered, pausing the show before standing up. “You know, you have feet that work- You can get your own damn sprinkles!” 

 

She yelled over her shoulder as she disappeared into the kitchen, leaving Agatha puffing out a little snort as she mumbled, 

 

“And yet, you’re doing it for me”

 

The woman continued to eat her ice cream, humming a soft tune as she watched Nicky bite and thrash around the small rope toy. Agatha had bought it for him the other night on a trip to Walmart with Rio. She made a sex joke out of the rope, of course. But overall, she was the one who spent way too much time in the pet aisles- finding things to spoil the boy with. 

 

Too busy in her own mind, she didn’t hear the front door open- Only noticed as Nicky jumped up and a high pitch singing voice rang in the air like a bell,

 

“ Yooo-whooo! Are you?” 

 

The woman stopped in her tracks, Agatha paused mid ice cream bite as she looked up to find a pair of redheads staring wide at her. She slowly put the bowl back down on her lap, hearing Rio rush back out with the sprinkles container shaking in the air. 

 

“Your servant brings you your precious sprinkle-”

 

Rio paused as her eyes caught the duo across the living room. She stopped talking, words cut before cutting into a shocked,

 

“Hey..guys”

 

Natasha and Wanda both nodded in sync, small grins as they returned the hello. 

 

“You forgot about dinner, didn’t you?” Wanda asked.

 

Rio pulled her lips back, shifting side to side while holding up sprinkles. 

 

“Ice cream for din-”

 

“I uh, I should go” 

 

Agatha started to stand up, but Wanda was quick to shake her head. She shoved the dish of casserole against Natasha’s chest, nearly hopping over as she rambled. 

 

“Nonsense! The more the merrier. Besides, another buffer to deal with the old grump here”

 

She gestured to Rio who only rolled her eyes at her. 

 

“Oh, I wouldn’t want to intrude”

 

Natasha shook her head. 

 

“Nonsense. Wanda made far too much food again-”

 

“Bad habit” Wanda shrugged. 

 

“Another person eating means less leftovers I’m stuck with for lunch all week” Natasha sighed. “You’d be doing me a favor”

 

Wanda scoffed, shaking her head. 

 

“Oh poor you,” She mocked. “Your wife makes sure you eat, what a terrible life you live”

 

Rio snickered, unable to hold back her amusement. 

 

“So!” Wanda grinned. “I’m Wanda, this is my wife- Natasha” 

 

The other woman gave a small wave behind her. 

 

“Who do we have the pleasure of meeting?” 

 

Agatha subtly looked over her shoulder, making sure Rio was fine with the situation. She only shrugged, silently saying it was up to Agatha on what she wanted to do. 

 

Without another second to waste, Agatha flipped her hair to the side. She held her hand out, a proud smile crawled upon her face as she said the name Rio knew would damn her for eternity. 

 

“Agatha Harkness” 

 

Wanda’s grin faded before it grew wide like never before. Natasha’s eyes opened, suddenly more energetic than how she showed up. They both glanced over to Rio who was playing with the sprinkles bottle, avoiding eye contact all together.

 

I’m so never hearing the end of this one. 

 

“Well..” Wanda shook her hand, nearly jumping in the air. “This is going to be a lovely night!”

 

That’s one way to look at it....

The Unexpected Dinner Led Us Back to 505

Chapter Notes

Switched to 8 chapters because I'm making 7 and 8 longer than just short chapters btw!!

See the end of the chapter for more notes

"Stop and wait a sec
Oh when you look at me like that my darling
What did you expect?
I'd probably still adore you with your hands around my neck
Or I did last time I checked

Not shy of a spark
A knife twists at the thought that I should fall short of the mark
Frightened by the bite though it's no harsher than the bark
Middle of adventure, such a perfect place to start"

“This is really good” Agatha complimented Wanda’s dinner, followed by a quick- “Wanda, right?”

 

“More like Gordon Ramsey,” Natasha smirked, replying before the other woman had a chance to do so. “Her cooking may be incredible, but she’s a vicious being in the kitchen”

 

Rio and Agatha chuckled as Wanda rolled her eyes. 

 

The group were sitting outside. The back deck table creaked with every movement, chairs rusted from the amount of time they had spent outside. Worn out, used and well loved. The sunset was turning dark into the early night, casting shadows around them. 

 

Wanda and Natasha sat next to each other on one side, Agatha and Rio straight across from them. The duo who knew Rio well wouldn’t voice it aloud, but after they left that night words would be said through gasps and laughs. They’d point out the obvious, find every part of Rio hysterical. 

 

From how she was nervously chewing at her lip more than her food. The way she tried to keep her eyes off Agatha, but failed miserably to do so. How Agatha sat beside her and Rio didn’t dare move a muscle. 

 

It was more than amusing to them both. They actually felt hope Rio wouldn’t be sitting alone like an old grump the rest of her life. 

 

“Ignore her completely,” Wanda said, putting on a soft smile right after. “But, yes. It’s Wanda”

 

Agatha nodded, holding her fork up in the air as if it was a champagne glass to raise a toast. 

 

“Well, Gordon Ramsey Wanda , you are quite the cook” 

 

Wanda shook her head over the nickname that had caught on over the years. Now adding on another woman to call her in. The others fell into a soft laugh, but Wanda quickly cut through them with a chirping tone. 

 

“Anywaaaaay!” She drew the word out, putting her fork down to clap her hands. “Less about me, Agatha and more about you!”

 

Natasha swallowed her food with a nod. “Mm! Rio’s told us you’ve worked at the university for a few years now?” 

 

Agatha paused mid bite, her fork lowering as a slow grin stretched across her face. She tilted her head, looking over to Rio who was sinking more into her seat, using the food to hide herself. 

 

“She’s talked about me? How interesting..”

 

Here we go.. Rio groaned in her mind. 

 

Agatha looked back over at the couple, asking a small, “Good things I’d hope?” 

 

Natasha puffed out a short laugh, Wanda shot a glare at her wife before snapping her attention back at Agatha. 

 

“Well-”

 

“Her worst enemy, right?” Agatha chuckled. 

 

“Um,” Wanda said, shaking her head. “More like-”

 

“Worst nightmare” Natasha shrugged. 

 

Wanda lightly smacked Natasha’s shoulder which only made the woman laugh harder. Agatha smiled, shaking her head as she lightly chuckled. 

 

“You don’t have to lie, Gordon-”

 

“I fucking love this chick” Natasha laughed. 

 

Agatha leaned over, nudging Rio’s arm with a smirk. “I am well aware of Professor Vidal’s so called hatred for me” 

 

Rio sighed, rolling her shoulders back as she swallowed her food before speaking, 

 

“In my defense-” She started. “You had been incredibly annoying since your first appearance”

 

“Had?” The three asked in sync. 

 

And suddenly, Rio hated all of them more than she ever hated Agatha alone. 

 

“I guess I’ve graduated from being annoying to-”

 

“Being insufferable” Rio cut off. 

 

“Hm, insufferable enough to be on your couch eating ice cream?” Wanda asked. 

 

“Oh!” Natasha perked up. “Insufferable enough to be her- What was it? Sprinkle servant?”

 

Rio groaned, grabbing her plate as she muttered under her breath, “I’m not being sober for this”

 

She pushed up from the table, storming off inside as the three women behind laughed amongst themselves. 

 

Embarrassment was taking hold stronger than ever. Rio scraped the leftover bits of her food in the garbage, nearly shattering the plate in the sink. She was thankful to have a few moments alone. A plan in action to find a beer, alcohol of any sorts to drown this entire night out.

 

This is..fuck. 

 

She popped the cap off, tossing it in the garbage before tilting the bottle back against her lips. The cold liquid ran over her tongue, down her throat. Rio could only hope the effects would hit her soon enough. Maybe not being sober would help her power through this.

 

Why am I like this? Rio wondered.

 

Shouldn’t she be happy her friends were getting along with Agatha? The entire dinner had gone by in what felt like two seconds. With her exes, dinners dragged on and on. Wanda always had something to say after, Natasha nodding along and making her own little comments. 

 

Rio always knew it’d be coming when the second dinner was nearly over or even worse, barely began. The two gave her a certain look that said,

 

“She isn’t the one” 

 

In which, okay- Fine. Maybe letting your friends have such a powerful, large impact on your dating life wasn’t for the best. However, it didn't happen. The two would’ve given her a look by now. The energy during dinner would have been awkward, slow. Unlike with Agatha, it was a dinner Rio had never experienced before. 

 

Agatha fit in perfectly with them. She kept up with the banter, the laughter was endless with her. Rio felt comfortable by her side, mesmerized by her perfect beauty. How she melted in, a puzzle piece that was found after being lost for so long. 

 

So..why the hell was she so embarrassed?

 

Maybe it was losing her well known reputation of hating Agatha Harkness. After all, stating something powerful and stubborn for three years straight. Arguing left and right giving her a chance to be a tolerable person in Rio’s life wouldn’t happen. 

 

Why am I-

 

“Rio..” 

 

And just like that, being alone didn’t last as long as she’d have liked it to. 

 

Rio groaned, shaking her head. “Don't start-”

 

“Agatha Harkness is in your house?!” Wanda whispered. 

 

“What about ‘ don't start ’ do you not understand?!” Rio exclaimed in the same harsh whisper. 

 

Wanda took care of the three dishes because of course- She offered to take Agatha’s plate. Knowing Wanda, she was going to bring drinks out and make sure to continue this night- drag it and Rio’s embarrassment farther along. 

 

“She's not only here. In your house. On your couch. Eating ice cream, but also- She’s wearing your fucking clothes!” 

 

Shit. 

As if this couldn’t get any worse...

 

Rio took another swig, shrugging her shoulders as she replied,

 

“Or, we just have a similar taste in fashion”

 

Wanda scoffed, a wide grin as she looked over her shoulder. 

 

“Rio, you’ve owned those grey sweatpants since you were twenty six. And! I bought you that hoodie!”

 

Agatha began to sing the familiar taunting song in her mind, 

 

Busted, disgusted, never to be trusted.

 

Another swig, longer this time- Almost tempted to down the entire bottle in one go of it to crack open another. 

 

She scratched the back of her neck, shoulders shrugging for what felt like the millionth time. Rio began to stammer her words, struggling to come up with an explanation for anything other than the obvious.

 

“I- Listen- Okay, she-”

 

“I- Listen. Okay, she!” Wanda mocked, shaking her head. “Don’t you lie to me! It’s clear as day! How else would you describe your known enemy in your house and clothes?!”

 

“We’re friends!” Rio said. 

 

Wanda laughed. “Oh my god- Might as well go with the old, they were roommates at this rate! God, you’ve always been a terrible liar”

 

Rio muttered a few curse words under her breath, leaning her lower back against the counter. She pinched the bridge of her nose, tapping fingers against the side of her beer bottle. 

 

“I just don’t get it..” Wanda sighed. “You two are obviously perfect together. Why do you keep lying-”

 

“We aren’t even together, Wanda..” Rio said.

 

It wasn’t a total lie, per say. They hadn’t necessarily discussed what was going on between them. It’d only been a week or so since their whirlwind of enemies to lovers-

 

Oh my god. I’m in a fucking cliche trope. Rio realized. 

 

Even worse to that realization? The woman who called it, nailed the hammer on the head, was the one to predict Rio’s future stood before her. 

 

“What do you mean-”

 

“We just aren’t!” Rio shrugged. “I’m pretty certain this is just some…fling, hook up sort of situat-”

 

Wanda gasped, hands flying up to cover her mouth as she started to bounce off the heels of her feet. 

 

“Oh for fucks-”

 

“Hook up?! Fling!?” Wanda whispered in a giddy tone. “You slept together?! Oh, I knew it! Wait, wait- How was it? Did you fuck her- She fuck you? Or-”

 

“Wanda” 

 

“Your dry spell is finally over! The curse has been lifted, oh my god!” Wanda laughed. 

 

The woman reached over, grabbing Rio by the shoulders, shaking her back and forth as if she were trying to rid all of Rio’s hesitations. 

 

“I need details, Rio. Like. A S A P!” She said. 

 

Rio shook her head, desperate to hide how her skin burned. The memory of Agatha’s body against her own. Her moans, words, voice a ghost in the back of her mind. 

 

She shook her head harder, muscles in her body tightening like a string being wound up- fighting against its hold. 

 

“Nothing to detai-”

 

“Rio Vidal, you haven’t had sex in God knows how long now. Give it up. Spill!”

 

Rio half turned to put the beer bottle down behind her. She covered her face with both hands, shaking her head as she groaned a muffled,

 

“Wanda. No..just-” 

 

“Oh my godddd” Wanda drew out the word, letting go as she placed her hands on her hips. 

 

The woman stepped back, giving Rio space to hide in her shell even more. A turtle inverting her neck, escaping the daylight into her own darkness. 

 

For once in Wanda’s lifetime, it was hard to completely read Rio like a book. She caught a glimpse of the embarrassment, possibly guilt for holding hatred so long. There were nerves mixed in as well. 

 

However, a feeling was trapped beneath the surface. Something that Wanda couldn’t exactly quite pin. Neither could Rio. 

 

Wanda nodded, deciding to lay off and give in to Rio’s demands of letting it go. She didn’t want to drop the subject, but she knew Rio well enough that pressing harder wasn’t going to do much.  

 

Although, Wanda wouldn’t give up that easily. Not without making Rio clarify her weak attempt at bullshitting away from the obvious, trying to make it appear it wasn’t as it seemed. 

 

“Fine.” Wanda said, her tone serious- a hint of frustration matching it. “So. You and Agatha. Just a hook up? Nothing more?”

 

Rio took in a deep breath, hesitating before she weakly nodded- forcing it into a stronger one. She rubbed her hands down her face, dragging her cheeks down before letting them rest on either side of her neck. 

 

Wanda narrowed her eyes, lips parting to argue, but Rio beat her before she could.

 

“Just… fuck buddies”

 

Wanda asked. “Nothing more?”

 

“Nothing less..” Rio replied. 

 

“Mhm..” Wanda hummed, not buying the reply for a second. “And why only that?”

 

Rio forced a laugh. Wasn’t it obvious?

 

Agatha didn’t want something more. In Rio’s mind, it was screaming on repeat louder day by day how this would inevitably end. This all could be one evil prank, a joke that involved pulling one over Rio. Revenge for hating her for three years. 

 

Rio had drowned them out, letting herself enjoy being in the moment. But like clockwork, Wanda was there to snap her into reality. Smack her out of delusions, bring her back to earth. 

 

“I’m not..” Rio shook her head. “I don’t want anything more”

 

Wanda had to restrain a laugh over that. It was a pathetic lie, Rio even knew her words were bullshit. All she wanted day by day was something more. 

 

Rio didn’t want Agatha to leave. She had a nightmare a few nights prior Agatha was in the arms of another woman. If you told her weeks ago that thought would make her feel sick, Rio wouldn’t believe you for a second. 

 

However, it was there. The fear of Agatha slipping away. She worried this would be a blip in her life. A brief moment that’d feel like a dream, something that almost never existed. 

 

Wanda sighed. “Rio-”

 

“No, I’m serious..” She said. “I- You know I can’t stand her. I haven’t in years. This is out of boredom. I’m sure it’s the same on her end”

 

Rio felt her heart ache with every word she spoke. A lie that kept on killing her slower than starvation ever could. 

 

“Why do you do this?” Wanda asked. 

 

“Do what?”

 

“You-”

 

Footsteps came through the backdoor, AGatha’s presence dominating the space as she always did with any room she stepped into. Rio’s eyes widened, panic striking through as she cleared her throat- grabbing her beer to take a significant swig from it. 

 

“Agatha, hey” Wanda smiled, appearing as if nothing was wrong. “We were just heading back ou-”

 

“Actually, I gotta go. Crisis date savior has been requested” 

 

She held her phone up, wiggling the device as she referenced it. 

 

Rio didn’t look to see the fake smile Agatha wore. She already heard it in her voice, her sudden departure that lined up perfect to get out of Rio’s home. 

 

The woman didn’t suggest to herself Agatha had overheard her. Instantly, her mind screamed how she regretted ever being here. This was it. The clock had run out, their time together was over. By Monday, things would be back to normal and this would cease to exist.   

 

“Oh, well..” Wanda sighed. “It was really nice meeting you. I hope we get to do something in the future! I know you’re dealing with a recluse here though. Getting her out of the house is like pulling teeth”

 

Agatha chuckled, but there was no warmth. Just a sound echoed into a void.

 

“I’ll uh, bring these back to you on Monday” 

 

Agatha referenced her clothes, but Rio didn’t pay attention. She just nodded, panic drinking from her beer as they all mumbled goodbyes to one another. 

 

The front door opened and shut. Rio felt the familiar emptiness fill her entire home. Even with her two closest friends still present, her beloved dog running around with glee- It was vacant. No life as if Rio had become Death, doomed to exist for eternity without any love or being around her. 

 

The woman was so lost in her solitude, ripped to shreds layer by layer- She didn’t hear Natasha walk in or see the look on her face. Only being snapped out of it with Wanda breaking the tense silence behind her. 




“What’s wrong?” Wanda asked. 

 

Natasha ran a hand through her hair, teetering side to side as she shrugged. 

 

“Pretty sure something may have been said in this kitchen that uh, said enemy did not like hearing” 

 

Wanda’s own heart broke, looking back over to Rio as she exhaled a long breath. 

 

Before she was able to say something, Rio slammed her beer down- Excusing herself to the bathroom, never hearing behind the low voices that blended in sync with one word,

 

“Shit”

 

Rio nearly tripped over her own two feet flying down the small hallway. The bathroom door swung open, nearly flying off the hinges and punching through the frame when she slammed it shut. Her back pressed against it, holding herself up the best she could. 

 

Her knees wanted to cave, body weakening into a messy pile of bones. A puddle of what she once was. The thought of Agatha hearing those words felt worse than Agatha not wanting her. Why was that? 

 

She always hated Agatha, never wanted her to be around, always shoved her away and-

 

Shit. I fucking love her. 



No, no. That couldn’t be it. How do you fall in love with someone you just hated days ago? 

 

Because, never actually hated- Yes, I fucking did- do! No- I-

“Ugh!” 

 

Rio groaned, pinching the bridge of her nose as she squeezed her eyes shut. If her thoughts kept having an argument of their own, Rio was sure her head would explode. 

 

Her silence in solitude wasn’t gifted to her for long. Which wasn’t surprising, not when Wanda was only down the hall from her. 

 

She didn’t knock, didn’t ask- Simply cracked open the door and stuck her head inside with a small smile. One that Rio didn’t bother to look at. Even if it was an empathetic sad one, a smile filled with understanding- 

 

Rio didn’t want to see it.
She didn’t want to see anything or anyone. 

 

Unless your name was Agatha Harkness, but..not even Rio would admit that. 

 

Wanda closed the door behind her, leaning against it as she whispered, “Looks cozy..”

 

Rio scoffed, turning the water on, letting the temperature run as cold as possible. She let her fingertip stay in the stream, unsatisfied until the sensation made her gasp from how frozen it felt. Only then did she bring both hands under to splash a good amount on her face. 

 

“Want a washcloth?” Wanda asked.

 

Cold water was always a tactic Rio used to bring herself back down from panic or emotional distress of any kind. Wanda would never forget finding her in the shower, frozen as can be when Rio thought she lost Nicky. (He was hiding in the kitchen cabinet where Rio kept her snacks) 

 

However, Rio shook her head as she turned the water off- stepping back to sit on the edge of the bathtub. 

 

She kept her eyes down, fiddling with her thumbs as she nibbled on her bottom lip. Wanda didn’t expect Rio to willingly speak to her. She prepared to fight and pry, annoy and pester until Rio either freaked out or kicked her and Natasha out of the house. Whatever it took, Wanda was prepared to do so. 


The woman ran a hand through her hair, taking in a breath to collect words, about to speak when-

 

“Do you think she heard?” Rio asked. 

 

Wanda snapped her head back up, eyes wide as she scrambled to redirect. Rio wasn’t one filled with surprises. She was someone who never went off script, always stayed the same. A routine that never changed. 

 

But now? 

 

Agatha Harkness has gotta’ be a witch.. Wanda thought to herself. 

 

“Um,” Wanda hummed, tilting her head side to side. “I mean..possibi-”

 

“Don’t sugarcoat it” 

 

Wanda scoffed. All of her sweet, tender, nice and soft caring demeanor was swept away. She put her hands out at her sides, snapping with a quick reply,
